Fujian Provincial Committee: Gao Dengting Discusses the Fujian Situation, His Escape, and the New Flag Design 71

(Nanjing) Gao Dengting, of the Fujian Provincial Committee, because he refused to echo the reactionary organization, came to Nanjing on the evening of the 26th. He went to Shibanqiao to meet Chairman Lin and report on the Fujian situation. He also met with Wang Jingwei at noon on the 27th. Within a few days, he will leave Nanjing to go to Jiangxi to see Chiang, reporting everything. Gao said that the brewing of the Fujian incident had been going on for months, but he did not expect it to advocate alliance with Russia and accommodation of the Communists. When the incident of the 19th was about to occur, because he did not casually support it, he avoided it by staying in a residence in Cangshan, across from Fujian, for several days and was monitored and searched. In order to avoid the dangerous situation, at dawn on the 23rd of this month, he climbed over the wall, injured himself, and took the China Aviation Company's Shanghai-Guangdong plane to Shanghai, arriving at noon that day. He has been recuperating and resting in Shanghai for several days and only took a train to Nanjing last night. It is now scheduled to meet with Wang Jingwei at noon on the 28th to report the entire course of the Fujian Incident in detail. After the meeting, he will leave Nanjing to go to Nanchang to see Chiang. Gao also said that because he did not join the actions of the people in Fujian, he felt unfree. He knew nothing else, but he once saw the design of their so-called People's Government's abolition of the party-state and the new national emblem, which was half red and half green, with a horizontal black line in the middle, and a yellow five-pointed star inlaid in the center of the flag. It is said that the five-pointed star represents the Social Democratic Party, the red symbolizes revolution, and the blue represents peace. A certain Shanghai newspaper reported the other day that their new national emblem was a right half red above and blue below, and a left half red, yellow, blue, white, and black five colors, which is inaccurate, because I personally saw the former. Gao also said that although the reactionary organization in Fujian Province has been established, its members are complex and there are too many internal contradictions. Although they are temporarily united at this time, he believes that they will eventually disintegrate. It is reported that the 19th Route Army has begun to differentiate internally. He personally speculates that it may be a rumor because the 19th Route Army previously had two factions, the Chiang faction and the Cai faction. However, it has only just been launched and will certainly not differentiate so quickly. Therefore, the rumor that Qu Shou-nian has led senior military officers to leave Fujian Province must be as unreliable as the previous saying that Cai Tingkai does not approve of the reactionary organization. The 19th Route Army originally had six divisions, which had not yet been replenished after suffering losses during the suppression of bandits, so they are short of their full complement. In addition, Weng Zhaoyuan's recruited bandits and Chen Guohui's old troops number no more than a few thousand. Their only attempt now is to peep into Zhejiang because they think Guangdong is not easy to attack, while Zhejiang is easier to capture. However, it is heard that the central government has heavily fortified the border between Zhejiang and Fujian and will definitely not allow it to be invaded. (27th Special Telegram)

Luo Jialun's Speculation on the Trend of the Fujian Situation 72

(Nanjing) At the memorial week of Central University, President Luo Jialun reported on the problem of the Fujian Incident. Standing on the perspective of a Central Committee member, his observation on the Fujian situation roughly meant that Chen Mingshu's temperament is different from others and he likes impulsive words and deeds. We can prove the cause of this Fujian Incident entirely by Chen Mingshu's impulsive instigation, not a purposeful move, based on his past behavior and words. Therefore, we can get three results when we speculate on the future trend of the Fujian situation today: (1) Because Fujian is adjacent to Japanese-occupied Taiwan, Japan will inevitably occupy eastern Fujian. (2) Because Fujian is adjacent to Jiangxi, the Communist Party will inevitably occupy western Fujian. (3) If the pseudo-government attacks Zhejiang to the north, the Communist Party will definitely enter southern Fujian; if it attacks Guangdong to the south, the Communist Party will inevitably enter northern Fujian. It will gain nothing from the occupation, and the 19th Route Army will be completely sacrificed, which is a pity. Finally, Luo also said that political changes in our country have always been related to a certain country. This Fujian Incident is certainly no exception. Before the Fujian Incident, there was Yano active in the north, and there was Yamamura active in Fujian. Therefore, the behavior of Li Jishen, Chen Mingshu, Chen Youren, and others is enough to destroy the country and more. (27th Special Telegram)

Reports on Two Memorial Weeks by the Central Government and National Government 75

(Nanjing) The Central Government held its 106th Memorial Week at 9:00 a.m. on the 27th. Dai Chuanxian, Chen Lifu, Li Ciwen, Li Zonghuang, Li Jingzhai, and other staff members, totaling more than 400 people, attended. Yi Chuanxian chaired the meeting and made a report, stating that after the Fujian Incident occurred, he felt that it was due to the lack of strong will and firm belief among the comrades of the party. Because of the lack of strong will, they are often instigated by others, and because of the lack of firm belief, they are tired of the revolution and the doctrine. If we want to save the country, we must eliminate this kind of mentality and take the legacy of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, trustworthiness, righteousness, harmony, and peace as the principles of self-cultivation and dealing with others. If comrades do so, the party will be united, and if the people of the country do so, the foundation of the country will be consolidated, and there will be no false clouds of rebellion and national subjugation. (27th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) The National Government held a Memorial Week on the morning of the 27th. Lin Sen, Shao Yuanchong, Zhu Jiahua, Chen Gongbo, Chen Shaokuan, He Yaozu, Wei Huai, Lu Chao, Li Yuanding, Zhang Ji, Lin Xiang, Niu Yongjian, and more than 400 staff members of the National Government attended. After Chairman Lin led the ceremony, Shao Yuanchong reported on the Fujian Incident, stating that this Fujian Incident is very serious. The most serious of the anti-revolutionary acts that have occurred in the past were Yuan Shikai's proclamation as emperor and Chen Jiongming's betrayal of the Premier. However, they did not go so far as to sacrifice the interests of the entire country to foreign countries. This time, Chen Mingshu and others advocated rebellion, not only betraying the party and betraying the Premier, but also selling out the entire Chinese nation. Huang and Zhao Return to Suiyuan From Bailingmiao, Huang Discusses the Main Points of Solving the Autonomy Problem, Zhao Talks About the Hundreds of Miles of Uninhabited Land in Bailingmiao 85

Suiyuan Correspondence, Huang Shaohong, Zhao Pilian, and others returned to Suiyuan from Bailingmiao at 4:00 p.m. on the 19th. In advance, the Chairman of the Suiyuan Provincial Government, Fu Zuoyi, the Commander of the 70th Division, Wang Jingguo, the Directors of various Departments, and representatives of various agencies all went to the Beisha Liang suburbs to welcome them. The army, military police, police, and military band all lined up to greet them. When Zhao Pilian's car arrived first, Huang Shaohong, Xu Tingyao, and others also arrived soon. They got out of the car at Beisha Liang, exchanged greetings with Chuan Zuoyi and others, and then took a car straight to the Suiyuan Hotel. The street was heavily guarded. Many people came to the province with Huang and Zhao, including the Zhasak and Shabazi of the Siziwang Banner. After Huang got out of the car and rested for a while, he met with newspaper reporters at the Suiyuan Hotel. In the evening, Fu Zuoyi set up a banquet at his private residence to welcome Huang and others. Xu Tingyao, having lived in Mongolia for a long time, went to Datong that night, and after visiting Yungang on the 20th, he returned to Beiping. The Mongolian-Han Joint Celebration Conference will be held within a few days.

Huang Shaohong's remarks roughly stated: "We waited in Bailingmiao and talked for a long time, conveying the Central Government's intentions one by one. We did not recognize any of their requests for a unified organization. The matter of dividing a province into autonomous regions has been accepted, with Suiyuan as the first autonomous government and Chahar as the second autonomous government. In accepting the principle, we must take into account the issue of the Central Government's authority. This proposition is still not affirmative and must be carefully considered by the Central Government and the Legislative Yuan before a detailed decision can be made. There will be no changes in the county governance problem. The defense problem has been studied based on economic principles, with the overall goal of not harming the interests of the Mongolians. We have sent personnel to various leagues and banners to conduct a detailed investigation of the animal husbandry industry, and there are no results yet. The Central Government intends to establish state-run pastures and private pastures to jointly seek improvement, which can also increase national income. All tax revenues that should be managed by the leagues and banners will be clearly divided to avoid confusion. The organization and expenses of the autonomous region government will be allocated by the Central Government. The location of its establishment has not yet been determined, etc."

According to Zhao Pilian's remarks, De Wang and Yun Wang canceled the Inner Mongolia Autonomous Government plan and proposed to establish autonomous governments in separate districts. A written report was submitted to your department. This is only a general decision and does not violate the plan set by the Central Government. According to the Central Government's plan, the Suiyuan and Wuyi League governments would establish Mongolian Political Affairs Committees in addition to the various departments. Now, De Wang and others have a new plan with different names, establishing the first and second autonomous region governments. The Chahar Mongolian banners will follow this example. De Wang and others' opinions will be conveyed to the Central Government, and there are many places that need to be specified in detail, etc. Zhao also said that Bailingmiao has hundreds of miles of uninhabited land. In such a vast area with so few people, everything is not easy to carry out. From Bailingmiao to Wuchuan, I felt like I was entering a prosperous area from a desolate place. Wuchuan is like Shanghai to the inland compared to Bailingmiao. Returning to Suiyuan is like walking into Paris! He couldn't help but laugh. (19th)

Guizhou Province's Attitude Towards the Fujian Incident丨Li Zongren and Bai Chongxi Have No Temporary Expression丨 86

Guangzhou Communication, since the Fujian incident occurred, Guangdong has decided to take the main purpose of securing peace and democracy. However, the attitude of Guizhou Province is extremely noteworthy to the general public. The southwest five provinces included in the Fujian situation, Guizhou Province actually occupies one of them, and Li Jishen is the chairman of the new situation in Fujian, which vaguely has the appearance of summoning the two Guangdong provinces. However, Bai Chongxi is relatively down-to-earth, first consolidating the internal affairs of Guizhou Province, and then linking with Guizhou, Yunnan, and other provinces to consolidate the foundation before developing northward. Now, the Fujian situation suddenly organizes a people's government, advocating equalization of land rights and realizing the acceptance of the Communists. Whether this kind of political program is approved by Bai is a major issue for Guizhou Province to develop northward. Moreover, since Guangdong has now expressed that it will not participate in the Fujian incident, the geographical situation of Guizhou and Fujian is blocked by Guangdong Province, which is also a barrier to the union of Fujian and Guizhou. Therefore, the timing of Guizhou Province joining the Fujian situation may not have arrived yet. Therefore, in recent days, those in Guangdong in the military and political circles of Guizhou Province have made explanations on the attitude temporarily adopted by Guizhou Province. According to Huang Heling, the former division commander and current Wuzhou Customs Superintendent of Guizhou Province, Li Zongren and Bai Chongxi, the deputy commander-in-chief of the Fourth Group Army, are still in Nanning. Other rumors are not true. The Guizhou provincial defense army, the three divisions of the current Seventh Army, are stationed in Guilin, Qingyuan, and Liuzhou, and the Fifteenth Army is in Youjiang, Nanning, and Pingdong. There has been no movement for several months, etc. In addition, Zhang Renmin, chief of staff of the headquarters of the Fourth Group Army, made a statement yesterday, saying that Commander-in-Chief Li Zongren has only returned to Guizhou for more than a month. Because he stayed in Guangdong for a long time last time, he has many things to deal with after returning to Guizhou. Moreover, Bai Chongxi was ill two weeks ago and is still recuperating. Most of the affairs are handled by Li. Recently, he planned to go to various places in the province to inspect the army, but he has not had time to go. Since the changes in the Fujian situation, Li may come to Guangdong in the near future. The saying that Chen Mingshu is the commander of the five provinces of Fujian, Jiangxi, Guizhou, Yunnan, and Guizhou is very bizarre. The recent Fujian incident has been made public, and Guizhou Province has not participated, which shows that the rumors some time ago were inaccurate. In short, Guizhou Province is now under the leadership of the Southwest Executive Department and the Political Committee in terms of politics and party affairs, and should take the propositions of these two agencies as its propositions, and there is no special expression. The interests of the two Guangdong provinces are closely related. At this time of changing situation, we can only unite and go to the national crisis together, and take bandit suppression and resistance to foreign invasion as our duties, and there is nothing else to talk about, etc. Zhang's remarks are like this, but it is not yet known whether he can represent the true attitude of Guizhou Province. (22nd)

Recent Developments Between Fujian and Guangdong After the Fujian Incident, Guangdong Troops Entering Jiangxi to Suppress Bandits Have Stopped Advancing, Troops Stationed in Chaozhou and Meizhou Are Building Large Trenches 87

Shantou Correspondence, the Fujian political change, Guangdong Province is adjacent to it, and the news has greatly affected the market. The economy has shaken as a result. Chaoshan is particularly close to Fujian Province. Silver firms have already started manipulating the market, rising and falling several times a day. Therefore, various rumors also arise as a result. The various troops that previously entered Jiangxi to suppress bandits have stopped advancing in Guangdong and Jiangxi. The so-called plan to attack Huichang and Junmenling is no longer discussed. The Third Army Headquarters moved to Meixian, which was originally convenient for taking into account the Fujian and Jiangxi borders. Such as Jiaoling, Dapu, Raoping and other counties adjacent to the Fujian border, and Pingyuan, Xingning, Heping, Lianping and other counties adjacent to the Jiangxi border, have all added large troops stationed, taking defensive measures against incoming invasions. The officers of various armies pay great attention to the development of highway transportation. For example, Huang Renhuan's plan for nine highways connecting Shanghang, Wuping to Songkou, Jiaoling, Pingyuan and Xingning has already started surveying. All residents within ten miles of the highway, regardless of male or female, have an obligation to be conscripted. Those who are conscripted receive a tea and meal fee of one dime and a half per day. The SanNan Road highway on the Jiangxi border has also been greatly developed recently, but there are very few vehicles. It takes about two days to arrive at Chaoshan from the Jiangxi border via Xingning and Fengshun. Shantou to Huizhou also officially opened on the 22nd. Due to the development of highways, military mobilization is very flexible. After the Third Army Headquarters moved to Meicheng, all the equipment was quite complete. The military medical office and the health team are located in the Zhendong Weaving Factory in Shuinanpu across the river. Shuinanpu is adjacent to Fengshun. Matoushan, Tongguzhang, and Yetian in Fengshun are all adjacent to Meixian. The mountains, ridges, cliffs, and rocks in the area are extremely rugged. The Guangdong army started to equip the defensive works a few months ago and spent hundreds of thousands of yuan, but they have not yet been completed. Now they are also conscripting civilians to rush to build them, and they must be completed by the end of this month. There are also considerable defensive works in Baxiang Mountain bordering Wuhua, Pantian Jiuhua Tian Dong bordering Chaoan, Tangkeng Luojiayu, Huizhai, and Wujingfu bordering Jieyang, and Shuikou, Baiye, Jingxin, Jiulongzhang, Douxi, and Ganxi bordering Xingning. The Guangdong army's deployment in the two counties of Mei and Feng is obviously targeting Fujian.

After the Third Army moved to Mei, Commander Li Yangjing was in the province due to business and did not follow the army. All the important duties of the army headquarters were performed by Chief of Staff Zhou Zhi. The two divisions of the army were assigned to the command of the Second Column, with Huang Renhuan responsible for the command. Chief of Staff Zhou has now been transferred to the province for another mission. Chen Jitang has separately appointed Ouyang Xin, deputy commander of the Eighth Division, to succeed Zhou as chief of staff and act on behalf of the Third Army. The Third Army has also established a rear office in Shantou to handle rear transportation and supply matters. Zhang Ruigui is responsible for maintaining law and order in all parts of Chaoshan.

The situation on the Fujian-Guangdong border is that due to the Guangdong army's strict suppression of bandits, most of the bandits and Communists have fled to Fujian and are hiding in various places. Only one regiment of the 19th Route Army is stationed in Zhaoan, Yunxiao, and Zhangpu counties, and the local militia has weak self-defense capabilities. For example, last month, the county seat of Zhaoan County was counterattacked by the Wushan Shen Donghai bandit gang, and the shops in the county seat suffered great losses. Party and government agencies and personnel of militia autonomous organizations all fled, and order gradually recovered after more than ten days. The mountains on the Fujian-Guangdong border stretch for hundreds of miles, and it is easiest to hide and gather bandits in the caves. Moreover, all bandit gangs contain Communist elements, and they must distribute leaflets and paste slogans whenever they cause disturbances, claiming to fight local tyrants. The 19th Route Army is stationed between Longyan, Zhangping, and Zhangzhou, and is unable to take care of everything. The Guangdong army stationed in Dapu is also inconvenient to intervene. Even if the two sides simultaneously attack, it is not easy in the thousands of layers of mountains. According to returnees from western Fujian, the 19th Route Army is stationed in Longyan, Shizhong, Hexi, Nanjing, and Zhangping, with three armies of Zhang Yan, Qu Shounian, and Shen Guanghan. Huang Renhuan's Guangdong army has entered Wuping, Shanghang, and Yongding with six regiments, but they are all like crossbows shooting tigers, and they will not fire easily unless the tiger comes. Longyan, above Liancheng and Shanghang, are bandit areas, or places where red and white intersect. Even the bandit areas that have been recovered have not been able to restore their original state to this day, because the original land contracts have been burned, the land slopes have been plowed, and the area of land has been allocated. Various people have been divided, and the control of physical labor, mental labor, and agricultural economy has become habitual, and it is impossible to restore the original state in any case. The output of rice and grain in the bandit area has greatly increased after the land was divided, and the output of bamboo paper in Changting has also sharply increased, but it has been blockaded by the national army and cannot be transported out. The bandit area lacks only salt, medicinal materials, ammunition, kerosene, and coal, etc. (22nd)

Jiangsu Province, Measures for Storing and Paying Clearance Special Funds, The Actual Number of Transfers Should Be Reported on a Weekly Basis, A Request Slip Should Be Prepared for Disbursement 88

Zhenjiang Correspondence, the Provincial Land Bureau believes that the total amount of clearance special funds collected by various counties should be statistically compiled to facilitate implementation, and the disbursement procedures should also be handled in detail to avoid misappropriation. Moreover, the clearance special funds of various counties are more important for the progress of land affairs, so it specifically, together with the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, ordered various county governments, it has been found that the Provincial Government Committee passed the regulations of this department on the custody and payment of provincial funds at the 606th meeting on October 31 of this year. , which is related to the clearance fees of various counties. After consultation between this department and the bureau, it was decided to implement it on December 1, and several points were stipulated as follows: (1) The collection agencies of various counties should report the actual number of clearance fees turned over to the treasury to the Department of Finance and the Provincial Land Bureau by week and month. At the same time, it should report to the County Clearance Fee Custody Committee for registration (this matter shall be handled by the accounting director, if not established, it shall still be handled by the county government) (2) Each county shall prepare a request slip for the disbursement of clearance special funds and submit it to the Department of Finance and the Provincial Land Bureau. The check shall be submitted directly to the Provincial Land Bureau for review, and the Department of Finance shall countersign it. The Provincial Land Bureau shall then issue it to the Clearance Custody Committee of each county. After the standing committee members have signed it separately, they shall pay it to the treasury. (3) The Department of Finance and the Provincial Land Bureau shall order the collection agencies of various counties to report the total amount of clearance fees collected up to November 30. The total amount of disbursements and the total amount of actual deposits shall be checked by the deadline. (4) All clearance fees collected and deposited shall be transferred to the treasury for storage by the end of November. In addition to separate orders, a copy of the provincial special fund custody and payment measures is hereby attached, and the county government shall comply with it. (November 27)

Vegetable Vendors on Daoqian Street in Suzhou Oppose Moving Into the Vegetable Market 91

Daoqian Street and Yuyuxiang near Xumen are busy commercial areas, especially the vegetable market in the morning. Recently, the county government built a small vegetable market in Xiliku and ordered the vegetable vendors there to move in together. The monthly donations are contracted by recognized merchants and levied on the vegetable vendors. However, the general vegetable vendors have never paid donations for business, and the business community there also believes that if the vegetable market is moved away, the business of oil, rice, wine, meat, southern goods, groceries and other stores will inevitably be greatly affected, so they immediately helped the vegetable vendors and opposed moving into the vegetable market. After repeated attempts to persuade them to no avail, yesterday (27th) Patrol Officer Li Yin of the 25th Precinct, under orders, persuaded the vegetable vendors to move into the vegetable market and at the same time prohibited street stalls. The shops along Daoqian Street immediately recruited general vegetable vendors to move into the shops to do business to show their resistance. Patrol Officer Li failed to exhaust his plans, so he prohibited the shops from setting up vegetable stalls and ordered them to move into the vegetable market to do business. Therefore, the merchants were furious and went on strike at 7:30, with signs on the doors saying that business was not free and they could only suspend business. The patrol officer had no choice but to report to the Public Security Bureau for instructions. The Inspector General Xu Jiarui arrived at the scene and mediated at the Daoyang Fire Brigade. He temporarily allowed the vegetable vendors to do business in the shops and persuaded them to open the market. The shops then opened the market at 9:00, but the vegetable vendors in the Yuyuxiang area who had moved into the vegetable market on the previous (26th) also moved out of the vegetable market and continued to do business in Yuyuxiang after hearing the news. There was no one in the vegetable market. The recognized merchant of the vegetable market felt that his rights were involved and would lose his capital, so he applied to the county government for relief.

Wuxi Bandits Continuously Rob and Injure People 92

In the fifth district of the county (Tianshang City), at Gaoxiang Lane in Xiwan, Chang'an Bridge, a villager named Gao Pan'gen, 41 years old, who works as a farmer, lives in poverty. Around 2 AM yesterday morning, six bandits suddenly arrived, each wielding knives and wooden sticks. They pried open the door and dragged Pan'gen from his bed, demanding he reveal the location of his hidden silver. Pan'gen replied that he had no money, which angered the bandits. They then pulled out knives and stabbed Pan'gen's right foot three times in quick succession. Blood flowed profusely, and he collapsed in extreme pain. Not satisfied, the bandits then broke into Gao Xi'gen's house, threatening him into silence. They also stabbed Gao's grandmother on her right wrist and other parts of her body. Subsequently, they rummaged through chests and cabinets, searching and looting at will. They stole over 200 yuan in silver that had been collected. After obtaining the loot, the bandits fled with loud shouts.

Changshu Wife Plots the Murder of Her Husband 94

Chen Jintang, a villager in the sixth village of Beixin Gate, Dongzhang City, in the tenth district of this county, is currently over 40 years old. He married a woman named Wang, who is over middle age but of a fierce disposition. Jintang is henpecked and fears his wife like a tiger. Besides farming, Chen also works as a cook. Whenever there are events nearby, Chen is hired to cook. The other day (the 25th) at night, Chen returned from cooking for a certain family, feeling a slight stomach ache, resembling sha. He immediately collapsed on the bed. Unexpectedly, his wife, for some unknown reason, flew into a rage, first scolding her husband severely, then conceiving a murderous intent. She went outside and grabbed a bamboo dustpan. Re-entering the room and seeing no one around, she seized the opportunity while Jintang was unprepared, slamming the dustpan on Jintang's neck and forcefully pressing down, killing him. Jintang screamed for help, but the event happened quickly. By the time his younger brother entered to rescue him, he had already died. The assailant, Chen Wang, was immediately apprehended. At dawn, the incident was reported to the Ninth Sub-Station of the Public Security Bureau, and the murderer was taken into custody. The district chief, Gui Shutang, personally reported the matter to the county. The county government will now dispatch an investigating officer to the village for an autopsy.

Jiangyin Telegraphs the Province Requesting the Abolition of the Education Bureau 97

Citizens of Jiangyin, including Feng Yuanzhang and Chen Tianjue, along with 128 others, have jointly telegraphed the Provincial Government's Department of Education, stating that since the establishment of the Jiangyin Education Bureau, it has wasted over ten thousand yuan annually, while educational funding has increased. Education is deteriorating daily, with the bureau serving as a superfluous and flawed entity, giving rise to numerous abuses. In terms of financial matters, the bureau has yet to submit its 1921 fiscal year report, while owing rural schools eight months' worth of fees. The Department of Education, to protect Jiangyin's education, dispatched four provincial supervisors, Yi Feng, Ruan Liu, and others, to Cheng to conduct a special inspection lasting three months. Their inability to promptly depart further proves the superfluous nature of the Jiangyin Education Bureau. Therefore, they earnestly request that the Jiangyin Education Bureau be promptly abolished and its functions be managed by a county-level department, thereby streamlining the system and facilitating supervision. The remaining bureau funds can then be redirected to educational initiatives, offering a glimmer of hope for Jiangyin's education.

An Incestuous Crime Occurs in JiaShan Jiao Diao Wan 101

A resident surnamed Wang, living in the 39th village of Jiaodiaowan Town, Fengjing East Village in Jiashan County, is sixty years old, and has two sons, the elder named Yingzhou, and the younger named Yuezhou. Both are married with children, their family is well to do, and their lives are filled with joy. Unexpectedly, Old Wang had a few drinks in town the other day. When he returned home, he was slightly drunk. He saw his two sons working in the fields, and did something inappropriate. Old Wang reprimanded them sternly. The two sons saw that their father was indulging in alcohol, and were disgusted. Therefore, Yingzhou pushed his father, Wang. Old Wang was old and weak, and fell to the ground. Yuezhou then struck Wang's vital parts with a farming tool, causing his immediate death. The mother heard the commotion and was extremely upset. Neighbors gathered and all were shocked. On one hand, the village police reported it, and the village chief reported it to the Jiaodiaowan police station, who sent the police to arrest the two murderers. The Wanxiang Arrives in Shanghai and Sails to Beijing This Morning 104

The Wanxiang steamer set sail from Mawei on the afternoon of the 25th and arrived in Shanghai at 1:30 PM yesterday, docking at Pier No. 2 of the Ning Shao Terminal at the Sixteenth Bund. Prior to the arrival, the Shanghai naval authorities, having received word of the Wanxiang's imminent arrival, dispatched two platoons of soldiers from the Naval Guard Battalion, accompanied by the Jiangnan and Jiang'an small steamers from the Jiangnan Shipyard, to protect the pier. The First District Office of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, along with the Criminal Investigation Team and the Water Police Bureau, also sent small steamers and detectives to the pier to provide security. Among the welcoming personnel were Chen Maoxian, adjutant of the First Fleet of the Navy; Ren Guanghai, Navy Staff; Chen Yongqin, captain of the Tongji warship; Chen Zaofan, deputy director of the Jiangnan Shipyard; Yu Qiaqing, manager of the Sanbei Company; Guo Yongrong, former director of the Fuzhou Public Security Bureau; and several dozen family members and friends of the students. At 2 PM, after the Wanxiang steamer docked, the welcoming personnel met Principal Du Xigui in the main cabin. Subsequently, Du disembarked and was transported by a Navy car to his brother Shenchen's residence on Fulu Li Road. The students remained on board, preparing to be transported to Nanjing this morning on the same steamer to study at the Capital Naval Torpedo Camp. Du will also escort them to Beijing this morning to report everything to the Ministry of the Navy.

Du Xigui Discusses the Current Situation in Fujian 105

This reporter met with Du Xigui, principal of the Naval Academy, aboard the ship and inquired about the situation in Fuzhou and his departure from Fujian. He provided a detailed account, stating, "We boarded the ship on the afternoon of the 24th and departed from Fujian on the afternoon of the 25th, arriving in Shanghai at this moment. The entire contingent consisted of 132 students and 21 faculty members. Upon departure, one student fell ill and was unable to travel, so he was advised to stay behind temporarily. Therefore, only 131 students came along. All school assets remaining in Fujian are currently being safeguarded by the garrison troops. In short, the Fujian authorities treated the academy very well this time. This was the result of my joint appeal with veteran naval elder Sa Zhenbing to Cai (Tingkai). Cai's original intention was that even the students' luggage and books could not be taken out. From now on, all faculty and students will only go to Beijing to study temporarily at the Torpedo School. The situation in Fuzhou remains normal. Naval institutions in the Mawei area can be said to be completely taken over, so there is inevitably a slight atmosphere of fear there. Governor He Gonggan has taken office. Mr. Sa (Zhenbing) is only presiding over local affairs in the capacity of a guest. Any external rumors of high-ranking positions are completely inaccurate. Currently, among the people of Fujian in Fujian, only Mr. Sa can speak with authority. The naval training camp has been completely disbanded, and most of the marines have been taken over. Those who have not been taken over are now moving towards the areas of Changle and Lianjiang. Commander Lin Bingzhou is currently in Sandu. When we passed the Changmen Fortress from Mawei, we did not see any Japanese warships stationed there. Huang Qixiang is indeed in Fuzhou, but I do not know the details of other important figures in Fujian because I have not met them." At that time, the reporter asked again if Fujian had communist leanings. Du said, "This is probably just talk. There are no real communists in China at all." After the conversation, he said goodbye.

Students Say the Navy Was Greatly Deceived 106

The reporter then selected one of the older students and inquired about the recent situation in Fujian. According to him, the entire student body of our school in Mawei is 132 students. Today, only one person did not come due to illness. The school was originally divided into four classes, two navigation classes and two engineering classes. The students came from all provinces, not just Fujian. For example, I graduated from the first class of the Nanjing Naval Training Camp and transferred to Mawei for further studies. Starting from the 22nd, troops were dispatched to guard the front and rear gates of our school, and no one was allowed to enter or exit. Later, after the principal negotiated with the authorities, Cai Tingkai issued a handwritten order allowing them to leave the school. Therefore, from the 24th, when we boarded the Wanxiang steamer, when students left the school, in addition to books, any slightly bulky luggage had to be inspected by the guards before they could be released. Therefore, from 1 PM until about 7 PM in the evening, the entire contingent completed boarding the ship. On the afternoon of the 25th, we left Mawei and passed the Changmen Fortress without being inspected. The commander of the Changmen Fortress is currently Yun Yinglin, but the gun levers of the fort had already been taken away by the Navy. Yang Tingying did have an appointment as Naval Commander, but he was only utilized by the Fujian authorities for one day. Yang then avoided the position and did not take it. The situation in the provincial capital is still normal, but the common people are not allowed to casually discuss politics. Anyone who does so will be arrested. The flags issued are red on top and blue on the bottom, with a yellow circle in the middle. They are mostly forced on merchants and civilians to hang. Today, on the same ship to Shanghai, in addition to our school's faculty and students, there are also about forty or fifty soldiers from the training camp and marines from other provinces. Because the soldiers of the training camp were disbanded by the Fujian army and had no place to stand, and a small number of marines, because they were registered in other provinces, were unwilling to be transferred to the Fujian army, so they changed their uniforms and secretly fled to Shanghai. In short, the Changmen Fortress, the Mawei training camp, and the marine corps were greatly deceived by the Fujian authorities this time. Because when the Fujian coup first occurred, the Fujian authorities declared that all naval institutions would not be touched. Later, as the Nineteenth Route Army gradually advanced, the various institutions in Mawei saw that the situation was not right and prepared to withdraw, but it was already too late. Fortress Commander Li Mengbin, at this tense moment, boarded the Jiangyuan warship and went to Sandu. Among the Fujian newspapers, only the Minbao, because it was run by the Japanese, slightly expressed central government opinions. All others were taken over by the Nineteenth Route Army, so their opinions are completely biased towards the Fujian authorities, etc.

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, sources close to Central Committee member Li Liejun told reporters from the Xin Xin News Agency yesterday that Li was deeply saddened by the Fujian coup and had sent a special representative to Fujian to investigate the truth. The Fujian coup is deteriorating daily, so Li's mediation, based on the current situation, is unlikely to succeed and can only be left to its natural course. Although the Central Committee members remaining in Shanghai have met frequently in recent days, they have not discussed the mediation of the Fujian coup because neither the central government nor the Fujian authorities have expressed any concrete opinions.

Yesterday, a reporter from the Guowen News Agency met with Central Committee member Xue Dubi and asked about Feng Yuxiang's attitude after being appointed chairman of the Fujian Provincial Economic Committee, and the attendance of the Central Committee members in Shanghai at the upcoming Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee. Feng Does Not Leave Shandong: Recently, I have still had frequent correspondence with Mr. Feng, inquiring about his recent situation. Since the Fujian coup, although rumors have been rampant and he has recently been appointed under false pretenses, Feng has not expressed any opinions on their actions, so there is no need to deny the rumors.

Fourth Plenary Session: The notice for the convening of the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee has been received. I am currently busy with legal affairs in Shanghai and have no spare time, so I am afraid it will be difficult to attend and I am not prepared to submit any proposals. Mr. Feng also has no intention of participating. As for the claim that the Central Committee members remaining in Shanghai plan to hold a joint meeting in Shanghai before the session, it has not yet been realized. Generally speaking, they are still in the process of contacting each other.

Replacement Aircraft Flight 114

Although the original pilot, Lumiere, has been discharged from the hospital, he still needs to rest. Six Passengers 115

After the Fujian Coup, Foreign Ships Dominate Freight Transportation. China Merchants and Ning Shao Ships Have All Been Suspended. Passenger Trains Operate as Usual, but Freight Trains Are Reduced. 117

Since the Fujian coup occurred, all Chinese ships operating on the Shanghai-Fuzhou line have been suspended and have stopped calling at Xiamen. Only foreign merchants continue to operate as usual, so they have monopolized freight transportation. The freight transportation of other ships and trains in various places has also been affected. The details are recorded below.

Chinese Merchants Suspend Service on the Shanghai-Fujian Route 118

The Chinese merchant ships operating on the Shanghai-Fuzhou route include the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Qinshun, the privately-owned Sanbei Company's Wanxiang, and the Chang'an Company's Hua'an. The foreign merchant ship is the Jardine Matheson & Co.'s Jiesheng. A total of four ships. Today, China Merchants Bureau's Taishun has stopped operating on the Shanghai-Fuzhou and Shanghai-Xiamen lines. Hua'an is now operating on the Shanghai-Tianjin line. The Sanbei Company's Wanxiang, after arriving in Shanghai from Fuzhou yesterday, decided to switch to the Shanghai-Hankou line.

Foreign Merchants Continue as Usual, Dominating Freight Transportation 119

The Jardine Matheson & Co.'s Jiesheng, which operates on the Shanghai-Fuzhou line, departed from Fuzhou the other day and is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai today. Due to foreign relations, it has been decided to operate as usual and is scheduled to depart from Shanghai on the first day of next month. As for the South China-bound ships of China Merchants, Sanbei, and other Chinese merchants, they have stopped calling at Xiamen. However, the South China-bound ships of foreign merchants such as Nissin, Jardine Matheson, and Taikoo continue as usual, so foreign merchants monopolize the freight transportation on the Shanghai-Fuzhou line and the Shanghai-Xiamen line. Chinese merchant shipping companies are therefore suffering significant losses.

Affecting Ship and Train Freight 120

After the Fujian coup, the China Merchants Bureau's Xinming ship operating on the Shanghai-Tianjin line, the Jiangyu and Jiangtian ships operating on the Shanghai-Hankou line, the Guangli ship operating on the Shanghai-Wenzhou line, and the Taishun ship operating on the Shanghai-Fuzhou line, a total of five ships, as well as the Ning Shao ship operating on the Shanghai-Hankou line, have all suspended their original routes due to busy transportation. As for the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo lines, in addition to the usual passenger services operating as usual, freight trains have also been reduced. Therefore, the freight transportation of both ships and trains has been affected.

To Relieve the Stagnant Sales of Domestic Wheat, the Executive Yuan Issued an Order to the Municipal Government for Proper Handling. 125

The Executive Yuan issued an order to the Municipal Government to properly handle the relief of stagnant domestic wheat sales, stating, "The Secretariat of this Yuan forwarded public letters from the Nanjing Municipal Government and the Ministry of Railways, the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Finance, and the Rural Rehabilitation Committee, etc., regarding the investigation of stagnant sales of domestic products and ways to relieve the situation. Based on the reports of various investigation teams, as well as the reports investigated by the Ministry of Railways' telegraphs to various railways, and referring to the reports investigated by the Ministry of Industry's telegraphs to various construction and industrial departments, as well as customs trade statistics, the overall situation is divided into investigation items, reasons for stagnant sales, and suggested solutions for submission to the authorities for review, etc. After being submitted to the 132nd Yuan meeting, it was resolved to be sent to the National Economic Council for reference, and to be sent separately to the Rural Rehabilitation Committee and the relevant responsible or related agencies for separate verification and handling. With regard to the increase in taxes on imported foreign wheat and flour, the Legislative Yuan was consulted, and with regard to the second recommendation, the Ministry of Finance and the provincial governments should be instructed to implement it properly, and the Ministry of Industry should dispatch special commissioners to investigate and contact the provincial governments at any time. The Rural Rehabilitation Committee will also telegraph various provincial people's organizations to report on excessive taxes and levies, in addition to sending separate letters of inquiry and orders. This order is issued for compliance with instructions and reporting."

Gasoline and Other Dangerous Goods: Transportation Temporarily Not Accepted; Railway Ministry Instructs Railway Bureaus to Comply 126

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus received Instruction No. 7411 from the Ministry of Railways yesterday, which stated: "Upon investigation, gasoline is a highly flammable liquid with varying flash points, ranging from approximately 55 to 100 degrees Fahrenheit. Its hazardous nature is significant. Therefore, the Ministry's list of general goods includes gasoline in the classification table for explosive and dangerous goods, accompanied by detailed provisions for special packaging and marking. Furthermore, Article 40, Item 5, of the General Rules for Freight Car Responsible Transportation also stipulates that explosives and dangerous goods are not included in the categories for which responsible transportation is undertaken. Now, based on a letter from the Nanjing Mobil Oil Company to the Ministry's Freight Responsible Transportation Committee stating that the Jinpu Railway does not handle responsible transportation for gasoline, while the Pinghan and Zhengtai Railways require billing as responsible goods and charge an additional 10% for freight, which seems inconsistent with the regulations, it is proposed to explicitly stipulate that gasoline is not subject to responsible transportation and to issue a notice to all railways to comply."

The approval from the North likely stems from the provisions of Article 40, Item 5, of the General Rules for Freight Car Responsible Transportation, which allows responsible transportation for kerosene and oil products. However, gasoline and kerosene originate from the same source, petroleum. Furthermore, the term "oil products" originally refers to various oily substances listed in Categories E, 7th, 8th, and 29th of the Classification Table for Explosive and Dangerous Goods. Therefore, the Pinghan and Zhengtai Railways may have mistakenly assumed that gasoline can be treated like kerosene or as oil products subject to responsible transportation. To resolve this misunderstanding and prevent divergent practices, the railways should temporarily cease handling responsible transportation for dangerous goods such as gasoline, motor spirit, and benzine, and no responsible fees should be collected. In addition to separate orders, you are hereby instructed to comply with this order." The bureau has already forwarded this instruction to the Traffic Department for compliance.

Shanghai County Government Ordered to Maintain Public Order and Announce Martial Law; Strictly Instructing Subordinates to Guard Against Reactionary Conspiracies; Implement Practical Precautions to Ensure Local Security 127

Ministry of Railways Convenes Meeting in Beijing; Private Shipping Companies to Participate in Intermodal Transport; Liu Hongsheng and Others Invited to Beijing the Night Before; "Tonghua" Arrives in Shanghai This Morning Fully Loaded with Cargo 129

Xinsheng News reported that after the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company began handling national water and land intermodal transport, various private shipping companies strongly advocated for participation. After the Implementation of Intermodal Transport on the Longhai Railway 131

Since the implementation of intermodal transport between the Longhai Railway and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company on the 20th of this month, the "Tonghua" ship loaded the first batch of intermodal transport cargo at the temporary wharf in Laoyao Sunjiashan, Haizhou, and returned to Shanghai at 3:00 AM the day before yesterday. Yesterday, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's radio station received a telegram from the "Tonghua" informing them that it is expected to arrive in Shanghai this morning, carrying 1,000 tons of cargo including peanuts, soybeans, melon seeds, and golden needles. Swire Shipping Resumes Guangzhou Service; "Xinjiang" Departs for Guangdong Today; Negotiations on Compensation for Miscellaneous Goods Guild 132

Swire Shipping Company's South China route has a total of thirteen regular merchant ships operating from Shanghai. Since the Guangzhou seamen's strike, the company's Shanghai-Guangdong liners have suspended service for nearly half a year, resulting in significant business losses. This reporter learned about the resolution of the strike last Tuesday. However, it was not reported because the conditions had not yet been signed by both parties. The following details are provided regarding the company's resumption of the Shanghai-Guangdong service and discussions on post-strike matters with the Hakka community:

Compensation for Losses 133

It has been learned that the Swire Shipping Company and the Guangzhou Seamen's Union signed an agreement to resolve the strike, with the company agreeing to pay the Seamen's Union 179,000 silver dollars. This compensation is solely for the Seamen's Union and covers various living expenses incurred by dockworkers during the strike. Workers on the "Wusong" and "Foshan" ships will be re-employed, but they must comply with the company's established rules. The strike officially ended on the 25th.

Resumption of Guangdong Service 134

The Guangzhou route, which had been suspended due to the strike, has caused immeasurable business losses for the company's thirteen vessels on the South China line for nearly half a year. Upon receiving notification of the strike's resolution, the Shanghai office immediately resumed the Shanghai-Guangdong route. The Guangzhou warehouses reopened yesterday, and dockworkers and barges resumed work as usual. Therefore, the Shanghai office ordered the "Xinjiang" to depart today on the first resumed Guangzhou service, carrying over 2,200 pieces of miscellaneous goods loaded by the Shanghai Guangdong community. The "Jinan" and "Zhoushan" ships have also been scheduled to continue to Guangzhou in the coming days, and the Guangdong community has been notified to resume loading as usual.

Guangdong Community Consults 135

During the strike, the most significant losses were incurred not only by the company but also by the Guangdong food, grain, medicinal material, and cotton cloth guilds. Goods had been locked in warehouses for a long time, preventing unloading, leading to economic stagnation and severe damage to the goods. Therefore, the merchants requested Swire Shipping to compensate for the losses incurred during the strike. Swire Shipping was unable to accept this request, so the grain guild convened a meeting at the Shenxiutang in this city the night before to discuss the matter. The decisions made on the spot were: (1) If Swire Shipping does not compensate the merchants' losses, the grain guild will not load Swire Shipping ships. (2) Any Guangdong goods transported by Swire Shipping ships will not be purchased. This intention has been telegraphed to various guilds in Guangdong. Anyone who privately loads goods with the company will be fined 5,000 to 10,000 yuan. Yesterday, the cotton cloth and silk guilds also joined the boycott and telegraphed various Guangdong communities in the Yangtze River ports, Qingdao, Tianjin, and other places for unified action. Therefore, the issue is very tense.

Chamber of Commerce Appeals on Behalf of Sanyou Industrial Company; Crippling Industry Will Inevitably Lead to More Unemployment 136

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce sent telegrams to the Executive Yuan, Judicial Yuan, Ministry of Industry, Shanghai District Court, and Jiangsu Shanghai First Special District Court of the National Government in Nanjing regarding the Sanyou Industrial Company's Yinxian Plant shutdown case, which has many practical difficulties after being ordered to be enforced by the court. Since its establishment, Sanyou Industrial Company has been engaged in the cotton weaving industry for more than 20 years. Unfortunately, its Yinxian Port Plant was destroyed by fire during the January 28 Incident in 1932, resulting in significant losses and making it impossible to reopen. At the request of the original workers, the case was submitted for arbitration, which has a mandatory nature. In terms of law, the effect of the arbitration is equivalent to a final judgment of the court, and there should be no room for change even if recourse is sought from the court. All three trials were rejected. However, the content of the arbitration reportedly requires the company to resume part of its operations within three months, with a minimum capacity to accommodate one-fifth of the original workforce. Before resuming operations, the company must pay the workers a pro-rata living allowance based on their original salaries. This decision is difficult to implement. First, capital is needed to start operations. Second, even if operations are started, operating at only one-fifth capacity is considered impermissible by those with factory management experience. Without capital to start operations, the one-fifth of workers must be maintained indefinitely with living expenses, even until old age. Even with common sense, it is known that this is not possible. The credibility of the law must be upheld, but it is also difficult to implement in practice. Therefore, those responsible for nurturing the people, protecting their livelihoods, and managing the national economy cannot stand idly by. Fortunately, most of the one-fifth of workers have voluntarily abandoned the rights stipulated in the arbitration, so the method of mediation does not require other solutions. It is only necessary to extend this to the entire one-fifth of workers with the same will. The arbitration also states that the remaining workers may be dismissed according to the original agreement, but when the Shanghai and Hangzhou plants hire new workers, they should give priority to hiring the dismissed workers. From a practical perspective, the company's Shanghai plant lacks capital and cannot start operations, and the Hangzhou plant is also owned by the company, so expansion is not easy. Therefore, the above proviso can be considered a formality in practice. Thus, the only means of executing the arbitration is dismissal. The arbitration states that the conditions of dismissal should be in accordance with the original agreement, so the provisions of the original agreement must be fully understood, and it is difficult to take them out of context. The agreement has an addendum stating that all articles must comply with the government's promulgated regulations, and if the government modifies them in the future, they must still be implemented according to the modifications. Therefore, since the implementation of the Factory Law and the abolition of the Shanghai Special Municipality's Workers' Retirement Treatment Method, the provisions for executing the arbitration dismissal should be based on the Factory Law. The purpose of the execution of the Factory Law should be to simplify things. The targets that the court should give to the dismissed workers are not problematic, and the court should base the method of calculating these targets on the overall consistent spirit of the Factory Law. Even for the sake of prudence, it should be submitted for interpretation once, or at least be determined by a trial judgment before being executed. If the number of these target properties and the content of the arbitration are clearly stated, then Sanyou Company would have no right to claim or litigate according to the law. However, in fact, it is not. Without removing the facts in dispute, the court hastily issued an order stating that from the day after receipt, the Yinxian Port Factory should resume part of its operations within 20 days, based on the notice to select workers to report to the factory on time, and entrusted the Jiangsu Shanghai First Special District Court to assist in the execution, ordering the company to pay more than 75,000 yuan according to the amount opened by the workers within 10 days, otherwise, the factory would be seized and auctioned for compensation. The maintenance of the credibility of the factory opening arbitration has room for mediation, but the credibility of a court order cannot be fully achieved. The severance pay in dispute has not yet been determined by trial judgment, and the court hastily executed it without considering the company's financial capacity to bear it or whether it contains prevarication, and only based on one party's claim, without trial judgment, which is not considered in the interpretation of the law. In short, national laws are originally intended to protect the interests of the people. If only the employer is protected, the employees, although harmful, can still survive. Conversely, if only the employees are protected, the employer, although harmful, how can the employees survive? Who does not sympathize with the unemployment of the Yinxian Port workers? Therefore, the legal provisions and interpretations may not be appropriate. If the Sanyou Industrial Company is sealed and auctioned, all of the company's operations will be shut down, and the number of unemployed workers will increase even more. The credibility of the court will be compromised, and the original intention of the law to protect the interests of the people will be fundamentally eliminated, which will have a significant impact on the national economy and the people's livelihood, directly and indirectly. Our association dare not remain silent. We hereby submit this telegram to your government's Executive Yuan and Ministry for review, (1) to find a way to make all one-fifth of the workers abandon the rights to restore the ministry permitted by arbitration, (2) the relevant court should legally try the decision of the Shanghai Special Municipality Labor-Capital Mediation Committee on March 14, 1929, and the subject of the dismissal grant in dispute, begging you to consider the fact that our country's industry cannot be crippled again, so that the number of unemployed people will increase even more, and the national economy and the people's livelihood will be fortunate, Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China, feels deeply grateful for the telegram. Seal.

The Two Railways Promote Domestic Tobacco; Reduced Freight for Lanzhou Water Tobacco; Hemp Packaging Charged at Third-Class Rate 137

The Two Railways Administration previously stipulated by the Ministry of Railways that boxed tobacco leaves should be charged at the second-class rate, and packaged tobacco leaves should be charged at the third-class rate. The North Ning Railway and other railways have generally charged the second-class freight rate for Lanzhou water tobacco due to its being boxed. The tobacco merchants complained that they could not afford the burden and requested a reduction or exemption. The Ministry of Railways then instructed the railways to investigate the packaging method of the water tobacco and whether it was charged at the third-class rate. The bureau now reports that, after investigation by the Business Department, Lanzhou water tobacco is a thick tobacco produced in Lanzhou, transported to Shanghai in boxes. Although the tobacco is coarsely processed, it is still raw goods, and most of the shippers are merchants who sell it. Each batch is only 300-400 kilograms and is packaged with hemp, so it is charged at the third-class rate according to the Ministry's regulations.

Sharp Drop in Cotton Yarn Prices; The Future Crisis of the Yarn Industry Intensifies; The Yarn Association to Hold Emergency Meeting Tomorrow to Discuss Measures to Save the Current Situation 138

Xinsheng News reported that after the Chinese Cotton Mill Association reduced its work hours, there was still a large amount of yarn in stock, and sales remained sluggish. The crisis in the yarn industry has not been reversed. Therefore, in order to jointly discuss ways to save the decline, it has been decided to convene a meeting of representatives from cotton mills across the country tomorrow afternoon to discuss the matter. Since the Fujian Incident, yarn sales have further decreased, and yesterday's market price drop was very severe, unprecedented. The findings are divided into the following sections:

General Meeting Tomorrow; In view of the intensifying crisis of the yarn industry and the urgent need to save itself, the Executive Committee of the Yarn Association decided a week ago to notify cotton mills across the country that an emergency meeting of cotton mills across the country would be held in Shanghai on the 29th and 30th to discuss rescue measures. Factories were requested to send representatives to Shanghai to participate in the deliberations. Representatives from various places have been arriving in Shanghai one after another since yesterday and are scheduled to hold a meeting at the Yarn Association at 2:00 PM tomorrow, and continue the discussion on the 30th.

Cotton Yarn Plummets Yesterday; According to a person in charge of the yarn exchange yesterday, the Chinese yarn market has been in a downturn since the "September 18 Incident," and the phenomenon has been deepening in recent days. The North China cotton yarn market has been gradually seized by the Japanese, and the Yangtze River area has suffered from natural and man-made disasters. The only areas that can be active are the Guangdong and Shantou Xiamen regions. Now that the Fujian Incident has occurred, once the situation expands, it will inevitably affect Guangxi and Guangdong, so the crisis will intensify. In recent months, the daily trading volume has been at most 400-500 bales, and in recent days, it has only been around 300 bales. Today (the 27th), the near-term and long-term market has been declining very sharply. The near-term November last price yesterday (the 26th) and today's (the 27th) final settlement fell to six yuan and nine jiao, and December also fell four yuan and eight jiao. The futures prices for January, February, March, and April all fell by two yuan and three jiao. As for the reason for the sharp drop, on the one hand, it was affected by the current situation. At the same time, in order to stabilize cotton yarn prices, the Cotton Industry Control Association sent people to take in more than 10,000 bales on Thursday, Friday, and Saturday of last week, so the near-term market price rose to 188 yuan, which was 6 yuan higher than before the purchase. Unexpectedly, today, 5,000 bales were suddenly released, causing panic in the market, and the decline was also straight down. It is said that there are currently more than 100,000 bales in stock in various factories.

Zhou Xiangxian Discusses the Recent Situation of the Yellow River Closure Project; The First and Third Districts Can Be Completed Within the Year; The Changyuan Breach is Currently Undergoing Diversion and River Dredging; Hope to Raise Cotton Clothing and Coal for Relief 145

Zhou Xiangxian, Director of the Engineering Team of the Yellow River Flood Relief Association of the National Government, came to Shanghai from Nanjing on the 25th to handle important matters and went to Beijing last night. A reporter from Xinsheng News visited Zhou at the Association's office yesterday and inquired about the recent situation of the Yellow River closure project. Zhou's replies are divided into the following sections:

Changyuan Breach 146

Zhou first said that the Yellow River breach closure project is divided into three districts. The first district, Henan Province, and the third district, Dongming County, Hebei Province, are both dry breaches (meaning there is no water at the breach), and the project is relatively easy to implement and can be completed within the year. The project in the second district, Changyuan County, with the 27th and 30th breaches, is very difficult to implement, and all efforts are being concentrated there. During the conversation, an aerial view of the Yellow River in Changyuan County, measured by the city's aircraft, showed that there was a lot of sediment accumulated at the turning point of the old riverbank south of the Changyuan County city. The water flowed straight north, forming two huge pools, and then rushed north to the Jin Causeway, forming the 27th and 30th breaches. The downstream river and the new river formed by the breach each formed a 90-degree angle, while the breach and the upstream river formed a straight line, which will inevitably change the course.

Closing the Channel and Opening the River 147

In order to close the mouth of the Jin Causeway, it is necessary to first cut off the water channels at the diversion point. There are four water channels. The first channel flows to the 27th breach, which has now been cut off. The second, third, and fourth channels flow to the 30th breach, and the second and fourth channels on both sides have now been blocked. Currently, efforts are being made to block the third channel in the middle. Some people say that the river is still horizontally overflowing and difficult to block, and that the slow progress of the project is not clear. In addition to cutting off the flow, two canals are also being dug in the newly flooded river channel turning point where sediment has accumulated, diverting the water from the two breaches, so that the sediment can be washed away.

Smooth Progress of Work 148

Currently, there are over ten thousand workers in various districts engaged in disaster relief work. They are paid wages for digging and filling earth for several days. Approximately three thousand workers are working in Changyuan. Engineering technicians are mostly concentrated in the Fengbao area, east and west of the breach. The progress of work in each district is very smooth. However, the diversion project must be completed before the ground freezes, as work will be difficult and may come to a standstill after freezing. Moreover, after the spring thaw, the water level will rise, hindering the work. Therefore, the work in the area has become very urgent recently.

Donation and Transport of Cotton-Padded Clothing 149

Furthermore, the disaster relief group of the association received a report from the Hebei Investigation and Relief Office stating that the office had raised 10,000 sets of cotton-padded clothing donated by the Beiping Xiao Hui School, as well as 1,000 sets of miscellaneous donations of cotton-padded clothing. In addition, General Zhu Ziqiao and others raised 500 tons of coal donated by the Zhongyuan Company for use by various weaving factories. The group immediately sent a letter to the Ministry of Railways requesting the Railway Bureau to promptly transport the relief supplies upon arrival at the station, recording the rice price as a precedent.

County Agricultural Education Center Actively Promotes Native Cloth Industry; Sales Greatly Reduced Due to Fujian Incident; Joint Research Association Formed by All Sectors 150

Zhang, the curator of the Shanghai Hemp Farmers' Education Center, recognizing the dumping of foreign goods, the bankruptcy of the rural economy, and the gradual decline of the native cloth sideline industry, which farmers have historically relied upon for their livelihood, has vigorously advocated for it for several years. The latest development plan for the native cloth industry is detailed as follows:

Expansion of Factories The center, in conjunction with various sectors, has established two native cloth factories in Touqiao on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway. Since their establishment, they have been producing dozens of bolts of cloth daily, and dozens more are woven by contracted farmers. However, to improve the quality of the products, they will be expanded and new machines will be replaced, which is scheduled to begin next year.

Promotion of Sales The large quantities of native cloth produced by the factories are sold by the native cloth store on Fenghua Road. The store's business relies on schools making uniforms and people from all walks of life making purchases to sustain itself. However, since the entry of foreign goods, monthly sales have decreased. Also, many schools still do not use native cloth for uniforms, and the Fujian Incident has impacted major sales in Fujian and Guangdong. It is planned to discuss and decide on a plan to promote sales in order to seek relief.

Establishment of a Research Association To improve the quality of native cloth, the center plans to form a native cloth research association in conjunction with native cloth comrades from all sectors, to engage in design. Preparations have been completed, and the inaugural meeting will be held within the next month.

Spring Exhibition The center's native cloth exhibition has been held in Shanghai several times. This year's exhibition at the Municipal People's Education Center attracted attention from all sectors. It is planned to hold a large-scale native cloth movement next year, with the exhibition to be moved to Zhabei.

Reduced Imports of Artificial Silk 151

In recent years, the sales of artificial silk have almost replaced natural silk. China's industry and commerce are lagging behind, and there are no domestic manufacturers yet, resulting in annual imports of more than 10 million taels. According to the recent four-year import statistics released by the International Trade Bureau, there is a gradual decline. The reasons are the daily drop in the price of raw silk and the increase in import tariffs on artificial silk. In terms of import volume, Italy ranks first, followed by Germany and Japan. In 1930, the total import was 127,091 dan, valued at 15,279,857 taels. In 1931, it was 133,491 dan, valued at 19,059,675 taels. In 1932, it was 103,388 dan, valued at 11,404,630 taels. From January to June this year, it was 46,234 dan, valued at 4,289,878 taels.

Garrison Headquarters Sentences in Liuhe Morphine Manufacturing Case: Each Sentenced to Five Months Imprisonment and Fined One Hundred Yuan 156

The Songhu Garrison Headquarters, based on a tip, dispatched an investigation team on October 8 to crack down on a morphine manufacturing facility in the Liuhe countryside. Only manufacturing workers Wang Agen, Bao Jitang, Chen Awu, Zhang Afu, and farmer Gu Fushi and others were apprehended. In accordance with the Anti-Smoking Law, Wang Agen, Bao Jitang, Chen Awu, Zhang Afu, and other four persons were sentenced to imprisonment. The main text is recorded as follows: Wang Agen, Bao Jitang, Chen Awu, Chen Afu are all found guilty of manufacturing opium substitutes, each sentenced to five months of imprisonment and fined 300 yuan each. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined shall be deducted from the term of imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. If the fine cannot be paid, it shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of one yuan per day. The raw materials and manufacturing equipment for opium substitutes, as well as transportation vehicles, shall be confiscated according to the list. The remaining perpetrators will be sentenced separately upon arrest. Gu Fushi, Yin Amo, Zhang Abao, and Wang Youwei are all found not guilty.
