The Assassination of Tang Jiapeng: The Assassin Recounts the Situation at the Time in Vivid Detail; Wang Jinkui Bribed and Instructed the Killing; How Tang Antagonized Others Has Not Yet Been Revealed 158

Tang Jiapeng, also known as A Yu, the former manager of Rongji at the Great World, from Ningbo, was shot and killed in front of the Great World at around 2:00 AM on June 18 of this year. The case was investigated by the special agency inspector Jin Jiulin and the patrol detectives of the French Concession, who successively arrested the assassins Zhang Tinggui, also known as Xiao Sizi (age 26), from Funing, and Zhao Guangfu (age 28), from Yangzhou, and sent them to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and investigation. As previously reported, the police have completed a detailed investigation. Yesterday at 10:00 AM, Judge Zhang Chaozuo presided over the criminal court and interrogated them. First, the police lawyer Fei Xizhen stated the investigation process, and Zhang Tinggui confessed that he had previously served in the Changzhou Garrison for about three months and then came to Shanghai to work as a rickshaw puller for seven years, living in the upstairs room of the overpass in Zhiheli, Hengfeng Road, Zhabei. On June 3 of this year, while I was pulling a rickshaw passing by the New Bridge, I met

Old Acquaintance Wang Jinkui 159

He asked me to go to Room 208 of the Asia Hotel at 135 Avenue Edward VII at 8:00 AM the next morning to discuss something. When I went there, Wang said to me that a friend of his had a feud with Tang A Yu, the manager of the Great World, and wanted to kill him. He asked me to find two people to help, and promised to give me a reward of 400 yuan. I agreed and went home. That afternoon, I went to the Hengfeng Road stove shop to find Zhou Er, a carpenter from my hometown who also pulled a rickshaw. After meeting, I told Zhou what Wang had said, and Zhou immediately agreed and said that he had a good friend, Zhao Guangfu, who is now in court. At 10:00 AM on the 5th, I went to the Asia Hotel again to report to Wang. At that time, there were five or six people in the room that I did not recognize. Wang asked me to wait at the corner of Avenue Edward VII and Rue Belles at 11:00 PM the next night, and then took me to Tang's residence on Rue Luzon

Wufuli Residence 160

He inspected it once and instructed me to go to the entrance of Wufuli at 12:00 to scout Tang's return time in preparation for attacking him there, and gave me 12 yuan for expenses. At noon on the 7th, I met Gu Dunyang, a rickshaw puller from my hometown, at the intersection of Hengfeng Road and Chang'an Road in Zhabei. I told him about this matter and invited him to participate. Gu also agreed and asked Gu to gather at my home in the evening. At about 1:00 AM, I went with Gu to the entrance of Wufuli on Rue Luzon to scout Tang's whereabouts. I did not see him for three consecutive nights. Later, Wang Jinkui asked to scout at the entrance of the Great World every night at 12:00, so I went with Gu. Wang pointed out Tang's appearance from the side. After going for three consecutive days, I saw Tang going home by car at about 1:00 every night. I immediately told Wang. Wang asked us to go to the Asia Hotel to

Discuss How to Kill Tang 161

Later, at 9:00 AM on June 15, I met Zhao Guangfu through Zhou Er's introduction at the Hengfeng Road tea house. Gu Dunyang was also present, and we agreed that Zhao and Gu would be responsible for killing Tang. I went to Wang's place every day to get three yuan for food. At 12:00 on the night of the 16th, I met Wang under the big clock opposite the Great World. At that time, Wang's accomplice, Sun Er, brought two pistols and distributed them to Zhao and Gu. We waited until after 12:00, but Tang was not seen. We returned the pistols to Sun Er and agreed to meet at the tea house at the corner of Longmen Road at 10:00 the next night. When the time came, I went to the Great World at 11:00. Sun Er still brought the pistols and handed them to Zhao and Gu. I stood at the entrance of the Great World as a lookout. Wang Jinkui and his friend Li Buwu stood opposite the Great World to watch. At about 1:00, Tang A Yu came out of the Great World and got into the car. Just as he was about to drive away, Zhao and Gu rushed up and aimed at the car. Zhao fired six shots and Gu fired three shots. When we saw that the purpose had been achieved, we fled to a tea house on Rue Beke that had been arranged in advance.

Wang Jinkui Was Already There 162

I returned one pistol, but Zhao did not arrive. Wang asked to meet again at the tea house the next morning. At that time, Wang paid 350 yuan, saying that because Zhao had not returned the pistol, 50 yuan was deducted. At 4:00 that afternoon, I invited Zhou Er to my home to distribute the money. Zhou received 85 yuan, Gu received 150 yuan, Sun Er received 40 yuan, and I received 60 yuan. I fled. Later, on October 27, I was arrested in Room 648, Haifang Road, and so on. Zhao Guangfu confessed that he lived in a thatched shed on Pu Road and had been in Shanghai for six years as a carpenter. At 2:00 PM on June 14 of this year, my old acquaintance Zhou Er came to my house and said that someone had asked him to kill Tang Jiapeng and invited me to participate. He promised to give me a reward after the matter was completed. I agreed and asked me to go to the Hengfeng Road tea house at 8:00 AM the next morning to talk. When the time came, I went and Zhou introduced me to Gu Jiaoyang and Zhang Xiaosizi, who are now in court. We

Planned the Killing of Tang 163

Zhao and Gu Dunyang took responsibility for shooting Tang. On the 16th night at 11:00, I went to the front of the Great World to meet Xiaosizi as Zhou instructed. I also saw a rickshaw pull up to the clock on the opposite side, took out a pistol and handed it to me and Gu to hold. We waited at the entrance of the Great World until after 2:00, but we did not see Tang. We returned the gun to the rickshaw puller and agreed to meet at the tea house at the corner of Longmen Road at 10:00 the next night. On the 17th night, I went as agreed. At 11:00, we arrived at the front of the Great World together. Before long, Sun Er still brought the gun and handed it to me and Gu to each hold one. We waited until after 1:00 and saw Tang coming out. Just as he was about to get into the car, Gu rushed close and fired six shots. I also stepped forward and fired three shots. The pedestrian who was killed was actually injured by stray bullets. After achieving our goal, we fled. The next morning, I went to Zhou Er to ask for a reward. Zhou said that I had to return the gun to get the reward. I refused and never saw Zhou again. On the 24th of the same month at 8:00 PM, I led people with guns and robbed them on Gordon Road. I was arrested by detectives and sentenced to three and a half years. Now I have been transferred to the case. The interrogation has come to a close, and the court has announced that it will be retried on December 4. The defendants will be returned to custody separately.

Upon learning of the indictment, he rushed back to Shanghai to turn himself in. After being acquitted, he also filed a lawsuit against Mackev and others for robbery, claiming that there were 11,175 US dollars, 722 British pounds, a bank passbook, and a check in his residence, all of which were robbed. Mackev and others denied it completely, so they filed a counterclaim against Morrison for false accusation. After repeated trials and investigations by the First Special District Court, it was ruled that both parties were innocent. The detailed process has been reported in previous newspapers. However, Morrison was not satisfied with the first-instance judgment and still hired a lawyer to appeal to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, stating various reasons and requesting that the original judgment be abandoned and that the defendants be punished according to law. Yesterday morning, the Second Branch of the High Court specially opened an investigation court to summon both parties for investigation. Mackev and others also hired lawyers to appear in court to defend themselves. Accordingly, both sides presented evidence and stated the facts of the case separately, and their words were mostly the same as in the first instance. The court then stated that the circumstances of the case were complicated and ordered an adjournment for further hearing.

It should be known that the distance between the old pier and the new pier is not short. If a new road is not built between the old pier and the Hefeng Factory, the distance from the new pier eastward to the Meifu Pier ferry is six miles. Businesses located at the old pier must travel back and forth, exhausted. Two-Headed, Four-Armed Monster 170

Ministry of Finance Responds to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Regarding the Tax Payment and Refund Methods for Stored Wine; Any Difficulties in Procedures Should Be Reported Separately for Further Consideration 173

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously received a letter from the Jiangjiu (soy sauce wine) Guild stating that the tax exemption period for stored wine had expired, and the tax bureau was about to conduct inspections, causing difficulties. They requested a telegram to the Ministry of Finance to exempt tax payments and refunds, etc. The Ministry of Finance replied, "Received the telegram. Regarding this case, the Ministry's Tax Affairs Department received a telegram from the Joint Association of Shanghai, Ningbo, and Jiangsu Wine Industries, relaying the same request from the Soy Sauce Wine Industry Guild. The Tax Affairs Department considered that tax payment and refunds for wine stored before the implementation of the new regulations were intended to clearly delineate boundaries and facilitate verification. Those that have already been opened, mixed, and sold in bulk are naturally exempt from tax payment. However, for those stored or sold in whole jars or transported, how can new and old be distinguished without tax-paid certificates? Therefore, tax payment and refunds should be uniformly applied according to the regulations to ensure consistency and avoid disputes. The department instructed the Jiangsu Stamp Tax and Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau to thoroughly inform the association and instruct all merchants to comply. All provinces are now following this procedure. How can Shanghai be an exception? In summary, the tax payment and refund for stored wine must be handled accordingly. If there are indeed difficulties in the procedures, the soy sauce wine merchants should report to the Tax Affairs Department and the Jiangsu Stamp Tax and Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau the total number of bottled wine, that has been bottled that paid old taxes in Shanghai that has not been sold, the number with public sale permits, and the number without permits, and the amount planned to be transported to other ports and the amount planned to be sold in this city. This is to determine the tax payment and refund methods for the benefit of both tax authorities and merchants. The request for exemption from tax payment and refund should not be discussed. You must immediately inform the guild to comply and avoid further delays. This is of utmost importance." This is the reply.

Telephone Bureau Responds to Wu Song District Municipal Committee Regarding Plans to Improve Telephone Service, but Time Is Needed 177

The Qihai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications replied to the Wu Song District Municipal Committee, stating: "Received your letter of November 23, stating that the telephones are dilapidated and waiting is required to speak with Shanghai. You requested that five more pairs of telephone lines be added between Song and Shanghai in the shortest possible time, and that all the old telephones currently in use be replaced with automatic ones. This is approved. Before January 28, the telephone in your town was originally commercially run and was an old magnet-type machine. Later, it was damaged in the war, and no one was running it. Our bureau took over to facilitate transportation, using copper wires to connect to Zhabei and establishing a branch bureau in your location. To date, there are only thirty-two subscribers. It would be uneconomical to convert to automatic machines. However, our bureau is currently designing and installing a 300-line automatic machine in the new city center area, which may be extended to your town in the future. The existing telephones are magnet-type, and although the components are old, the sound seems clear. However, the existing lines are insufficient, and to call the concession telephones, you must go through Zhabei and then to Nanshi to transfer, so the routes along the way are all related. Our bureau is now expanding the Nanshi and Zhabei relay lines from thirty pairs to fifty pairs, which will be completed in about two weeks. However, the lines to the concession are limited. In the past, the Chinese area called the concession telephones an average of about 3,000 times a day. Since our bureau included the Chinese-concession call fee in the monthly rent, the number of Chinese calls to the concession has increased to 11,000 to 12,000, which is three times more than before the merger, resulting in congestion at the '0' manual switchboard and inability to answer calls in time. Although we have notified all subscribers not to abuse the concession telephones unless there is an emergency to avoid hindering the calls of other subscribers, it is still ineffective. To improve telephone service, we have already ordered an expansion of equipment costing more than 100,000 yuan, but it will not arrive until next spring. The relay lines between Jiangwan and Zhabei have already been purchased and are being installed. However, the telephone lines between Zhabei and Wusong are often cut and stolen, several times a month. This year, there have been more than fifty cases. Our bureau has repeatedly sent letters to the Public Security Bureau and offered rewards for the arrest, but it has not stopped. Our bureau's loss is a small matter, but it is very laborious to send workers back and forth for repairs. The obstruction of traffic and the impact on the sensitivity of telephone service is one aspect. Regarding the relay lines between Song and Shanghai, our bureau is reporting to the ministry to find ways to increase them, that is, to transfer them from Jiangwan. In response to the letter, we hereby send a reply for your information."

Overturning a Kerosene Lamp Caused a Fire That Burned More Than Forty Thatched Houses 180

In recent days, the weather has been dry, so fires have been frequent, especially in the Zhabei slum. A group of disaster victims are haggard and have nowhere to stay, which is pitiful. However, at 1:15 a.m. yesterday, a fire broke out again near Qiwu Road, West Baoxing Road, Zhabei. The houses there were all thatched, and the residents inside were all coolies and rickshaw pullers. Shen Chen, a native of Jiangbei, was a widow and lived there. She relied entirely on her own labor for her livelihood. After she fell asleep the night before, she forgot to turn off the kerosene lamp. During a turn, she knocked the lamp over, and the kerosene spilled on the straw, causing the fire to ignite. It immediately spread to the whole house. She woke up in a dream and realized that it was too late to save the situation, so she ran out and shouted for help. The neighbors nearby also woke up from their dreams and scrambled for their lives. The order was in chaos for a while. The fifth district's police station was reported and immediately dispatched police officers to suppress the situation. At the same time, they notified the Zhabei fire brigades to rush fire trucks to the scene to put out the fire. However, the wind was strong, and the flames were soaring, making it difficult to start for a while. At the same time, the fire spread rapidly, and the thatched houses around became fire pits. Later, after the firefighters bravely rescued the situation, the fire was slightly reduced at about 2:30 a.m. It was not until about 3:00 a.m. that all the fires were extinguished. After the investigation, a total of more than forty thatched houses were burned down. Shen Chen, the person who started the fire, was taken to the ninth district police station for questioning and temporarily detained for further investigation.

Counterfeit Coin Operation Broken Up on Republic Road 183

Chen Alin, a 22-year-old Ningbo native and former cook living at No. 3 Xinyi Village, Pushi Road, in the French Concession, has been unemployed recently. On the evening of the 10th of this month, he bought a loaf of bread for one cent at the Speer's food store at No. 688 Avenue Joffre. Chen paid a dollar and the Russian gave him five 20-cent coins and a 10-cent paper note as change. Chen took advantage of the Russian's turning around to switch to the counterfeit coins he was carrying and told the Russian that the change was counterfeit and insisted on exchanging it. The Russian refused and called the police from No. 687 Avenue Joffre. The police arrested Chen and took him to the police station. Chen was nervous and threw the five 20-cent coins given to him by the Russian into an alley on the side of the road in an attempt to absolve himself of guilt. The police found four of them and took them to the police station. Later, Chen confessed that the counterfeit location was in the pavilion room at No. 551 Republic Road. Detective Liu Kunbao immediately took Chen to No. 551 Republic Road and arrested Gu Rongqing (33 years old), a native of Huzhou, and his concubine Du Chen (35 years old, native of Qingpu) on the third floor. They also seized three sets of the latest new Sun Yat-sen model and one set of the old Yuan Shikai model, one set of the 20-cent model, batteries, files, pliers, and other tools for manufacturing counterfeit coins, as well as counterfeit dollars (six new versions and four Yuan Shikai), seventy-six counterfeit 20-cent coins, and a piece of raw lead in the pavilion room on the second floor. They also arrested six men and women in total, including Cao Yixin (44 years old, native of Nanxun), Hu Baolang (35 years old, native of Chongming), and Zhang Linjiang (51 years old), and took them to the police station for interrogation and investigation by the Second Special District Court. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Zhang Chaozuo continued the trial in Criminal Court One. First, Attorney Fei Xizhen of the police station explained the police investigation process and prosecuted the defendants for manufacturing and using counterfeit coins in accordance with Articles 211 and 212 of the Criminal Law. Then, the Russian Speer testified about Chen Alin's exchange. Gu Rongqing admitted that he had been making counterfeit coins for several months. Chen Cao Hu and Zhang confessed that they had been selling and using counterfeit coins. Du Chen confessed that she had known Gu for only a month and did not know about the counterfeit coin manufacturing. After verifying the confessions, the court ordered the defendants to be remanded in custody and scheduled a verdict for the 30th.

Plot to Defraud American Oranges Exposed 184

The Fusheng Fruit Shop at No. 8 Wuchang Road had twenty boxes of American oranges worth 160 yuan stored in the Maocheng Cold Storage Company's refrigerator at No. 40 Huangpu Road to prevent damage. Recently, Jiang Zhongming, an apprentice from Anhui, who had resigned from the same industry, learned of this and came up with an idea to forge a Fusheng letter and seal at an engraving shop. At 2:30 p.m. on the 25th of this month, he wrote a delivery note, stamped it, and hired Shen Sanbao, a rickshaw puller from Tongzhou, on Wusong Road to deliver the note to the company to pick up the goods. Lu Zhengsheng, the bookkeeper from Ningbo, noticed that the seal on the note did not match and called Li Qikang, the manager of the Fusheng Fruit Shop from Ningbo, and found out that there was no such thing. He detained the rickshaw puller Shen Sanbao and learned that a young man surnamed Jiang had hired him to wait near the Great World on Avenue Edward VII. After a while, Li Qikang, the agent of Fusheng, arrived with Detective Zhang Guisheng of the Hongkou police station. They loaded the 20 boxes of American oranges onto the car according to the note and asked Shen Sanbao to push them to a parking lot near the Great World. Jiang Zhongming arrived happily and was arrested by Detective Zhang and taken to the police station. He was sent to the Third Court of the First Special District Court yesterday morning. Attorney Zhang Tianyin of the police station stated the situation and said that the defendant claimed at the police station that the matter was instigated by Xu Abao, who was at large, and that he was told to transfer the American oranges to the Ximolu vegetable market for sale. The note was presented for inspection, followed by testimonies from Li Qikang, the head of the cold storage company, Lu Zhengfu, and the rickshaw puller Shen Sanbao. When questioned, the defendant gave vague answers. Judge Xiao Xiefen ordered him to be remanded in custody and rescheduled the trial to investigate and verify the matter.

Buying Pork; Argument Over Small Amount Leads to Bloody Incident; Customer Leaves Happy, Shop Assistant Slashes Old Boss 187

The Shen Chang Fresh Meat Shop, located at No. 1252 Lujiabang Triangle Street, South City, is opened by Lin Caifa from Ningbo. It has been in business for several years and has a flourishing business. At about 10:00 a.m. yesterday, a customer came to the shop to buy several pounds of fresh pork. Li Axiao, a shop assistant, cut it, weighed it, and handed it to the customer. The customer felt that the pork he bought today was different from the pork Lin Caifa usually bought, and he complained that it was not worth the price. At first, he negotiated with Li Axiao for a long time, and even wanted to return it, saying that the pork was too expensive and demanding the money back. While the two were negotiating, Lin Caifa arrived and persuaded the customer. He also added a little fresh pork, and the customer was happy and left the shop. After the transaction was completed, Li was angry with Lin because the boss did not care about the shop assistant's face and only knew how to please the customer. So the two argued again. After people persuaded them, Li suddenly wanted to resign, and the conflict broke out again. Li was so angry that he slashed Lin's head with a meat cleaver. Lin was injured and fell to the ground with blood all over his head. Dong Shidong, the guard of the 24th post there, heard about it and rushed to the scene. He arrested Li Axiao and took him back to the first precinct, first station. Yi, the police chief, ordered Li Axiao to be interrogated and ordered him to be detained temporarily, pending investigation of Lin's injuries, so that he could be sent to the police station for interrogation. It is reported that Lin Caifa's injuries are serious and may be life-threatening.

Liang Shaojiu Industry Executive Committee 189

The Shanghai Liang Shaojiu Industry Guild held its 16th executive committee meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:00 p.m. The following matters were resolved: (1) The procedures for registering and renovating rejected alcohol are complicated, and transportation in this street is often mistakenly detained by the police. A summary was drafted and submitted to the Shangbao Branch for a request. However, there has been no practical approval to date. It is now decided that the previous four representatives will go to the inspection office on the 27th to discuss simplified methods. (2) To rectify the industry regulations, we should join the various alcohol industry groups and jointly submit a request to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to convene a temporary representative meeting of various industries in order to achieve it. The industry's account放賬should be sorted out first. For example, if someone owes money to Jia Hang for a long time, the guild should be notified and all members should be notified not to do business with them until they have paid off their debts in order to protect their capital and avoid indiscriminate 放賬. However, those who pay now are not subject to this rule. (3) Alcohol shops have permits, annual taxes, and permit taxes, so they only need to pay a retail license for tobacco and alcohol license taxes. Now, the tax collection office has repeatedly increased the taxes and harassed them. It is planned to submit a request to the competent authority for explanation to avoid duplication and ease the burden. At the same time, all businesses should be notified to exchange the receipts printed by the tax collection office for formal licenses as soon as possible to avoid being suspected of colluding when checked by other agencies and being punished for no reason.

Contribution of the Construction Industry 196

China's construction industry has progressed from wood and stone to reinforced concrete. The composition of reinforced concrete depends entirely on yellow sand and gravel. Therefore, for solid construction, one must first seek firm yellow sand and gravel. The gravel produced by the Songjiang Hongcheng Crushed Stone Factory has been certified by the Engineering Bureau to be firm. Compared with other gravel that is manually mined, loose in texture, and contains mud, it is vastly different. General draftsmen, engineers, and construction companies who seek solid and perfect construction in large-scale projects will find that the factory's products can fulfill their wishes. ▲ Welfare Company Men's Winter Coats at Bargain Prices The Welfare Company on Nanjing Road and Sichuan Road is now entrusted by a certain bank to sell European-made, finely crafted winter coats. The Nine O'Clock Dance Troupe Arrives in Shanghai for Performance 202

The Nine O'Clock Dance Troupe is the latest artistic group of Hollywood's standard beauties. They formed this group because they were a little tired of life on the screen, and they specialize in modern song and dance. Because of their exquisite art and beautiful looks, they have a reputation for being contemporary. Every performance draws crowds. In the summer, they travel with song and dance, their route being Tokyo, Japan, Shanghai, China, then south along the sea, from Siam to the East Indies, and then back to the United States. They have been performing in Tokyo for more than three months. According to reliable sources, they will arrive in Shanghai today and will perform at the New Light Theater in this city on the 30th. The program is very precious, and the songs and dances are all new works by famous artists, not the common tunes heard on the street. They will perform at the New Light Theater in this city, limited to one week due to travel arrangements. After the week is over, they will leave Shanghai. Moreover, because the songs and dances they perform require a lot of energy, they are inevitably tired. Therefore, they will only perform one show at 9:15 p.m. every evening.

Foreign Paris: Progress of the Chinese Painting Exhibition (2) 207

On March 3rd of this year, Mr. Xu Beihong and his wife, Ms. Jiang Biwei, brought their works to France to prepare for the opening. However, due to a lack of funds, all progress was met with unlimited difficulties. Fortunately, Beiping Sino-French University wired two thousand yuan, and Minister Gu and his wife each donated one thousand yuan, which allowed them to barely arrange everything and keep their promise to the French, which was also a fortunate event.

The Baomu Art Museum is divided into two floors, the lower floor being too dark and the space being very narrow, while the upper floor is the opposite. Our Chinese art exhibition was held on the upper floor. The arrangement was divided into ancient and modern sections. The two rooms on the left were for very ancient paintings, the central room was for near-ancient paintings, and the three large rooms on the right were for contemporary paintings. There were a total of 180 contemporary paintings and calligraphy, by 71 artists, as mentioned earlier. Now, the situation of modern and ancient paintings is briefly described below:

The so-called near-ancient paintings are the works of Ren Bonian, Shen Nanpin, Yu Zhiding, Qian Zai, Zhang Xi'an, Ji Gu, and Xu Dazhang, brought to France by Mr. Xu Beihong, totaling eleven paintings, which were displayed in a special room as representatives of the transition of ancient and modern art. The ancient paintings were works from the Tang Dynasty to the late Ming Dynasty. This part was entirely managed by the French, so the works of the Qing Dynasty were also included, which was quite mixed. There were twelve pieces of Song Dynasty murals, borrowed from Mr. Lu Qinzhai, a Chinese antique dealer, and other various paintings and Zhou Dynasty steel elephant, totaling 74 pieces, all borrowed from the Louvre and Guimet Museums, and collectors from France and Belgium, such as Mrs. LangweilLecerf·Valdo-Barley, Coleporter, Hyde, and Mr. Stoclet, Riviere, Vever, Culty, KelekianMallonVignierHenraux, Nubar-Bey, Rateau, Gerard. According to statistics, there were eleven ancient artifacts from Dunhuang discovered by Mr. Bo Xih, and one piece of Drunkenness, collected by Stoclet (the most famous collector in Belgium), six works from the Song Dynasty, eleven from the Yuan Dynasty, twenty-six from the Ming Dynasty, and seventeen from the Qing Dynasty.

Reorganization of the Anhui Education Department 208

(Anhui News) The internal organization of the Anhui Education Department still follows the old system of the 17th year of the Republic of China, divided into three sections and a secretariat, with a property management office set up outside. The responsibilities of the sections and shares reorganized by the fourth share of the first section are completely divided by business category. Therefore, the first section is in charge of funding and appointments, regardless of the funding and appointments of middle schools and social education institutions. However, other matters of secondary schools and other matters of social education are handled by the second and third sections. Although there is a division of labor, there is ultimately a lack of connection. Now, the department plans to change the method and plans to use the enterprise as the standard for dividing sections. For example, if the second section is in charge of secondary education, then all funding, appointments, and other matters related to secondary education will be managed by the second section, and so on for the other sections. Whether this kind of organization is convenient to implement remains to be seen after implementation.

China Boy Scout Specialist Qualification Training Standards (4) 209

(35) Plants 1. Able to describe the relationship between plants and life. 2. Able to draw the cell structure of plants with a microscope and make more than five experimental reports. 3. Know the growth and reproduction of plants. 4. Understand the respiration and photosynthesis of plants. 5. Able to collect and identify 30 kinds of leaves and 40 kinds of flowers and plants, and also be able to state the uses of leaves, stems, roots, flowers, fruits, and seeds for life, and give one example each. 7. Able to give one example each of the following plants and explain edible plants, medicinal plants, poisonous plants, spice plants, timber plants, fiber plants, dye plants, and ornamental plants.

(36) Sewing 1. Know the cutting methods of ordinary clothes and the types of needles and threads. 2. Able to cut a set of Boy Scout shirts and pants. 3. Able to sew or machine-sew a set of Boy Scout shirts and pants or a personal tent. 4. Able to weave and patch damaged clothes.

(37) Measurement 1. Able to make a detailed map with a scale of 1:2500. 2. Able to make a sketch in the field or from memory in a short time. 3. Able to measure height using various methods. 4. Able to measure the width of a river in the field. 5. Able to measure the distance between two inaccessible objects. 6. Know the uses of compasses, scales, contour lines, and specified symbols.

(38) Radio 1. Able to make a simple diagram showing the wiring method of the antenna, ground wire, and tuning coil, coupling device, coil variable device, detector, fixed and variable capacitors, receiver, etc. of a radio, and be able to explain the function of each component. 2. Know the structure, principle, and function of a triode vacuum tube. 3. Know the advantages and disadvantages of three kinds of antennas and the lightning prevention method for ground wire installation. 4. Know the use of batteries and over-electricity. 5. Able to make a mineral or vacuum tube radio by oneself and be able to use it practically. 6. Able to check the obstacles of the radio and the method of repair. 7. Able to send and receive Chinese Morse code at least eight words per minute or English Morse code at least thirty letters per minute. 8. Know more than ten international wireless abbreviations. 9. Must serve in a radio station for one week.

Sports Jiangda Football: Jinan Defeated Central Yesterday 丨Two to Zero丨 A Small Disturbance Occurred in the First Half: Luo and Li Collided and Were Sent Off: Jinling Defeated Daxia Six to Zero 214

(Nanjing, 27th) In the Jiangda Football Championship, Jinan and Central played at Zhongda at 2:30 p.m. on the 27th, with Yu Jie as the referee. Jinan is the holder of the Jiangda football championship, and it was expected that Zhongda would not be its strong opponent. After the start of the game, Jinan's offensive was very fierce within 35 minutes. Zhongda took a defensive stance. Although dangerous balls were frequently seen in front of Zhongda's goal, they were able to turn danger into safety due to their effective resistance. Unexpectedly, while they were competing with each other, Li Disheng was penalized with a twelve-yard penalty. Jiang Lianggui was unable to defend, and Nandong opened the scoring. Not long after the restart, Li Disheng and Luo Taoguang kicked Li's chest with one foot because of mutual competition for the ball. Fortunately, Li changed his hand and held his thigh, like a wrestling match. Li pounced directly at Luo, and the audience shouted in unison. The order was in chaos. After a few minutes, the referee sent Li and Luo off the field together, and the game continued. At the end of the first half, Jinan led by one to zero. After the break, they changed sides to fight, and both sides had ten players on the field. Although the Jinan team drove all their troops to the front line to attack fiercely, the Central University's defense was even stronger. After a long stalemate, Xu Yahui shot a goal two minutes before the end of the game. The momentum was very weak. It happened that Jiang Lianggui was leaving the goal to catch the ball, and the ball rolled into the goal in a smooth way, so Jinan took the lead again by one to zero in the second half. As a result, Jinan defeated Central by two to zero.

The Chinese Team in the International Race Walking Event Abandoned Team Participation: Only Ten Individuals Will Participate This Year 丨Resolved by the Race Walking Committee Yesterday丨 217

The Chinese Race Walking Association held a committee meeting at Murhall last night. Six committee members, including Shi Youhui, Yu Zichen, Zhou Yuyu, Zhang Zaojiu, and Lu Yutian, attended. More than 20 people attended, including Zhang Zhihe, Lü Chongyi, Ai Jieke, Zhang Xianlun, and Xu Aichen. After discussion, the following was unanimously resolved. The Race Walking Association has followed the National Sports Association and is actively preparing for the 50,000-meter race walking event at the 1936 World Games, without any slackening. It has been actively practicing since September of this year, and will practice the entire 50,000-meter course in 1935. This month happens to be 17 miles, so regardless of any changes or shortening of the course, those who have joined the practice are all advanced. Zhou Yuyu, Shi Jinsheng, Zhou Ruquan, etc., who have represented the Chinese team, have completely different steps from the 17-mile race, hoping to develop strong leg strength in order to seek further training. The performance of the newcomers is also remarkable, but they inevitably lack experience and are not very stable. Moreover, our Chinese team has won the championship for five consecutive sessions since 1928, which is a rare achievement and one of the most glorious events in the history of international sports. They are unwilling to lose it rashly. Moreover, the experience encountered during last year's competition is heartbreaking to talk about. Foreigners seem to be jealous of our Chinese team's continuous championship wins. Every athlete is strictly monitored from beginning to end, and they almost suffered a setback, but outsiders do not know it. Today, the racecourse refuses to lend to us Chinese because we are orderly, and their contempt for the Chinese has reached its limit. Therefore, in view of various relationships, our Chinese team seems to be able to abandon team participation in this session and only join individuals, limited to ten people. Because Mr. Beesliy, the general manager of the International Race Walking Association last year, restricted the participation of our Chinese, the ten people selected have correct postures and there is no need to be nitpicky, such as Lü Chongyi, Zhang Zaojiu, Xu Aichen, Chen Liwen, Lin Qiu, Yao Yaying, Lü Wenxia, Zhang Xianlun, Zheng Chengshan, and Cai Zhengyi. The registration fee will be paid by the team. As for the introduction staff, they have been changed to promotion staff in this session. Being behind the athletes is useless, and our Chinese do not need it, so we will not invite the so-called promotion staff.

Special Article China: An Overview of Modern Educational Thought (8) Lecture by Shu Xincheng, Notes by Sun Yucai 238

The thought of Production Education: In Chinese history, there was only the education of governance. Although the "New Education" originated with an emphasis on production, when transplanted to China, all science, engineering, agriculture, etc., became the so-called "foreign eight-legged essays" (a derogatory term for rote learning), and were used as tools for successful governance. However, after seventeen years, due to the severe panic of the world economy, China's market was naturally contested by the great powers, and the domestic industry was increasingly declining due to the economic aggression of the great powers. The international trade lending tables could not be balanced, and almost everyone could feel that the education of governance was of no benefit to the country. Thus, educational thought shifted from governance to production, and the advocacy of production education greatly increased.

The thought of Rural Education: After the May Fourth Movement, various political and economic theories and doctrines were imported, stimulating the Chinese people to pay attention to practical social problems. Rural education was gradually valued by educators. After twelve years, the Jiangsu Provincial Normal Schools and the Henan Provincial Normal School established rural branch schools, gradually engaging in practical movements. In 1927, Xiaozhuang School in Nanjing was established, opening a new era in the history of rural education. In 1930, many university education colleges established rural education courses. In 1931, the Shandong Rural Construction Research Institute was established, further increasing the strength of rural education. In terms of thought, although there have been many proposals in recent years, they can be summarized into only two theories: (A) the theory of rural life transformation and (B) the theory of rural construction. Each has its own sufficient new insights, but the goal is to jointly promote the development of rural education, with no differences. The spirit of practical "doing" is admirable.

The thought of Mass Education: In 1927, the National Government unified China. According to Mr. Sun Yat-sen's legacy of awakening the masses, mass education gradually became one of the contents of party-based education. In theory, it was vigorously promoted, and in practice, considerable achievements were made. We believe that the most effective were the China Association for the Promotion of Mass Education, which promoted mass education in Dingxian, Hebei, and the Jiangsu Provincial College of Education, which promoted mass education in Wuxi. These two places can also be regarded as representatives of educational thought. However, they were all educators who believed that mass education was a way to improve rural areas, and they attached great importance to its effectiveness, believing that it was "transcendent, thorough, fundamental, capable of solving personal life problems on a small scale, and capable of correcting people's hearts, changing customs, reducing internal strife, and harmonizing all nations on a large scale."

The thought of National Rejuvenation Education: After September 18th, due to the pressure of foreign invasion, the Chinese people's recognition of nationalism further increased. Academics discussing the issue of national rejuvenation also increased daily. Theoretically, the more systematic ones are Luo Jialun and Zhu Jiahua. Luo advocated creating an organic national culture to save China's current crisis. The most important meanings of the so-called organic national culture are two: (1) everyone must have a common intention to revive the Chinese nation; second, the efforts of various parts of the culture must become mutually coordinated under this intention. The method is the four words of sincerity, simplicity, heroism, and grandeur. Next, Zhu's theory is described. Zhu was the Minister of Education at the time. After September 18th, his sense of national rejuvenation was particularly keen compared to others. In July, he announced the short-term elementary school curriculum standards, which focused on restoring the national spirit. The Ministry-compiled textbooks could also be practically achieved. On December 1st, he issued an explanation from the Ministry of Education to come and reorganize the country's development together, further detailing the purpose of national rejuvenation education. He said, "China now, as a whole nation, must pay attention to national rejuvenation in education, and then the Chinese nation can be free. The Chinese national rejuvenation must depend on educators having two things: (1) cultivating the national concept of the people, (2) restoring the national self-confidence of the people." It is a pity that there is still no concrete plan for implementation.

Page 13

Spring and Autumn

Literary Inspiration 239

—

What is literary inspiration? No one has ever seen it, but everyone who is often engaged in writing always feels that there is such a thing in the world, and it is an extremely mysterious thing. Although wealthy and idle people will never need it, for the poor scholar, it is truly an indispensable treasure.

The ancients once said: "Literary inspiration comes mightily, like a gushing spring." Using spring water to compare literary inspiration is truly accurate! It is something that can be used endlessly. Sometimes, when excitement and joy reach their peak, it is like a sudden mountain torrent that arrives unexpectedly, allowing you to pick up your pen and write straight down without any obstruction. The good skills of writing ten thousand words while leaning on a horse are truly possible. But sometimes, when the weather is dry and the land parched, and the water source suddenly dries up, even if you hold a writing brush in your hand, and have ground the pine soot ink until it is fragrant and placed it in front of you, or even sit in a very comfortable rocking chair, and close the door of your study, you are still unable to find literary inspiration. No matter how much you rack your brains and ponder, you are still faced with a blank sheet of paper. At this time, it is as difficult as having to chisel a mountain to find water when there is no spring. Even if you smoke cigarettes like crazy and chew candy indiscriminately, it will only be for the benefit of your mouth and tongue. To think that literary inspiration can be ignited by this means is absolutely impossible!

I have another feeling. (Perhaps others do not feel this way, or even feel the opposite of me, then I cannot interfere, but I always feel that way myself.) The presence or absence of literary inspiration is not something that the writer themselves can control. In moments of joy and happiness, it seems that literary inspiration should be at its most uninhibited and flourishing, but often the opposite is true. In moments of sadness and anger, it seems that writing is impossible, but in reality, it often stimulates your literary inspiration, allowing you to write extremely good articles when you are not expecting it. The ancients often said: "Writing poetry and prose becomes skillful after hardship." This is truly correct! Others say that whether writing is smooth or not should be based on the person's knowledge, but this is because they do not understand or recognize what literary inspiration actually is. We must know that literary inspiration is definitely not the same as money. With money, you can buy drunkenness and laughter and do whatever you want. With literary inspiration, you cannot control it. It is absolutely automatic and absolutely mysterious. When it does not gush out, it does not matter how much knowledge you have!

The Modern Old Woman 240

— Jun Ti

Shanghai is the birthplace of modernity, and also its concentration point. You walk onto the street, and you can see the modern beauty of animate and inanimate objects everywhere. Of course, only the modern beauty of animate beings can stir your heartstrings and captivate your soul; but there is also a type of modern animal that gives you a strange feeling.

You often see a kind of woman, who has cut her hair, put on makeup, wears glasses, puts on a cheongsam, and wears leather shoes. This is indeed modern. But you first suppress your feelings, and then take a closer look, and you know that her hair is already gray, her skin is already wrinkled, her eyes are already dry, and her waist is already bent. And her feet are still three-inch golden lotuses, like a crescent moon. Looking at the way she walks, it's even more wonderful, not swaying gracefully, but staggering. Really, she doesn't want to stagger, but wants to learn to sway gracefully, but because she is burdened by her small feet, she is unable to do what she wants, so she has to stagger, and has to sway. She is indeed an old woman.

When I see this kind of modern animal, I can't help but shudder. I don't know what others think? What about herself? But in any case, she is modern, and yet an old woman; I dare not ignore the facts, so I give her a noble title: Modern Old Woman.

But if you look around, modern old women are not only on the streets, but also in the world. It (the world) has already implemented democracy, but kings and dukes still exist; it has already opened schools, but private schools still exist; it has already worked hard on construction, but thatched sheds still exist... There are still endless things to say. Her image is very similar to what you see on the streets, with different tunes playing the same melody. Alas? Is this modern? It's simply a contradiction!

Alas! Modern old women! If you cut your hair, you still have to apply some black oil; if you put on makeup, you still have to heal the wrinkles; if you wear glasses, you still have to add some sparkle to your eyes; if you wear a cheongsam, you still have to straighten your hunched back; if you wear leather shoes, you still have to enlarge your small feet. Don't just focus on modern trends, and forget that you are old, so that people who see you shudder, that would be stronger than eating vegetarian food and chanting Buddhist scriptures.

The Forbidden Standard of Beauty 241

— Yu Renwei

In the film industry of Hollywood in the United States, there is a special group of people who don't care about anything else, but only work on the female stars. It is said that they spent more than a year studying an ideal standard of beauty; if anyone meets this evaluation standard, she can be called the world's standard beauty. This strict standard includes a certain height, waist circumference, thigh thickness, buttock size, weight, and skin tone. However, until now, Hollywood has not found their so-called ideal standard beauty.

I say that these people are really idle and have nothing to do, so they do such meaningless things. Not to mention that it won't be found in a corner of Hollywood in the United States, even if you search all over the world for a lifetime, it will be in vain. Moreover, the standard of beauty can only be imagined, not determined; the ideal beauty in my mind may not be the ideal beauty in your mind; in the tropical regions of Africa, the uneducated black people, their women, in our eyes, not to mention being beautiful, are simply ugly and somewhat frightening, but in the minds of African natives, they may not be their ideal standard of beauty.

Let's talk about the beauties of our China. From ancient times to the present, quite a few have been produced. However, because of the changes of the times, the standard of beauty has also changed. The standard beauty in the eyes of the ancients was a frail, melancholic, and sentimental Lin Daiyu-style consumptive beauty; in today's 20th century China, due to the gradual influence of Western culture, modern men and women want to learn some foreign styles in everything. The consumptive beauty of ancient times has obviously been eliminated with the trend, and the barefoot girl of the wild rose type is rising in due course. Although some women do not have a strong physique at all, it is good that science is now developed, and they can be transformed artificially. Moreover, makeup items are readily available. The beauty of their hair, needless to say, can be taken care of by the barber; the beauty of the buttocks can be created by wearing high heels; the beauty of the breasts can be decorated with rubber fake breasts; the rest, such as the snake-like twisting, can be graduated within ten minutes, so now there are simply standard beauties all over the streets in the city, our poets probably won't write about "the mantle of birth" anymore!

A Visit to Xu Yang's Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition 242

— Tian Shoucheng

Mr. Xu Shiqi and Ms. Yang Manhua held an exhibition of calligraphy and painting works at the Youth Association on the second floor of Eight Immortals Bridge yesterday. Mr. Xu is good at painting, and Ms. Yang is good at calligraphy. They are a loving couple, which can be said to be the beauty of both, and it is difficult to combine both, so their collaborative works are truly precious. I took a car to watch yesterday afternoon and saw the walls filled with beautiful things, which were overwhelming. At that time, Mr. Ye Gongchuo was also there, and after browsing, he sighed and admired it. There were also many viewers who made purchases on the spot, and Mr. and Mrs. Xu treated them with great care and humility. I still remember that I met the loving couple in Lai'ai, Belgium, when our country participated in the Belgian Exposition three years ago. At that time, the two gentlemen each used their strengths to help the work of our country's representative office a lot, and we expressed our deep gratitude, and we especially admired the spirit of cooperation between the two gentlemen. Later, I returned to China, and Mr. Xu went to Germany to study modeling, while Ms. Yang studied in Paris. Each of them made achievements and returned with satisfaction. Now Mr. Xu works in the Health Department. In addition to his busy official duties, he must pick up his pen every night. I heard that most of his works are completed under the lamp. Not to mention his hard-working spirit, but I see his works, and he is good at both Chinese painting and Western painting. The flowers, plants, figures, birds, and animals he paints are all reaching the realm of perfection. And his wife is proficient in all styles of calligraphy, including regular script, cursive script, clerical script, and seal script. Each is extremely wonderful, and the brushstrokes are vigorous and not like those of a woman in her boudoir, which is very rare. Is this what is called a genius?

Chapter 19: Desiring to Be Together Yet Wanting to Part, Remembering Past Events in the Same Car; Half-Crying, Half-Smiling, Leaning on a Pillow, Sick in the Lingering Autumn

Or should I buy two tickets? He said he was going to Haidian, that was a lie. What would he do in Haidian? Visit his brother and sister-in-law? He hadn't made a fortune yet. Send Gui Zhi home? Their relationship wasn't good enough yet. But since he had promised to go to Haidian, he certainly couldn't not go. Otherwise, it would appear that he was deliberately lying. So he bought two tickets and took Gui Zhi to the bus together. The body of this long-distance bus was very high. But when Gui Zhi came to step on the bus door, she was a little short, and after trying twice, she still didn't get on. Ji Zhi was still at the bus door, and couldn't help but reach out and pull her onto the bus. At that time, Gui Zhi didn't think about it and grabbed his hand. (251)

Lip Reading Invented in Paris 244

We usually only know that fortune tellers use bone reading and palm reading to judge a person's good or bad fortune. Recently, spiritual scholars in Paris have invented lip reading. They divide the shape of the lips into six types: the first type is round lips, which expresses arrogance and a strong sense of self-esteem; the second type is semi-circular lips, which proves to be fanciful and indecisive; the third type is flat lips, which is full of emotion and most greedy for lust; the fourth type is pointed lips, which expresses various deep desires; the fifth type is oval lips, which is full of adventurousness and laziness and close to artists. We may as well use a mirror to look at our own lips to see which type they belong to and whether they match what is said above.

Mr. Beauty Contest 246

The city of Adana in Turkey organized a Mr. Beauty contest. The qualification for contestants is that they must be unmarried. The judges are young women. The method of judging is for each judge to record the beautiful points of the contestants' eyebrows, eyes, nose, mouth, ears, and other five features, and vote for a public evaluation. If they win first place, in addition to receiving a reward of 20,000 yuan, the most beautiful woman in the city of Adana will also be married to this person. It is said that in the previous competition, the most beautiful man was a barber who had not even graduated from elementary school, and the most beautiful woman was a famous writer and artist whose father was a high official.

A Man Who Hasn't Slept for Sixteen Years 247

Recently, a person suffering from a strange disease died in a hospital in Budapest, the capital of Hungary. His name was Shi Bian Kaili. During the World War, he served as an army captain and was very brave. Because he was frightened by enemy bullets on the battlefield, his spirit changed greatly and he could not sleep. Although he took strong sleeping pills, he could never fall asleep. It is said that he has not slept for sixteen years. After he died, the hospital dissected his brain nerves and carefully studied the cause of his insomnia.

Female Europe 248

According to recent statistics, the number of women in the capitals of European countries is generally greater than the number of men. In Berlin, there are 1,177 women for every 1,000 men; in London, there are 1,149 women for every 1,000 men; in Vienna, there are 1,169 women for every 1,000 men; in Paris, there are 1,195 women for every 1,000 men; in Warsaw, there are 1,185 women for every 1,000 men; and in Budapest, there are 1,192 women for every 1,000 men. Only in Rome, the capital of fascist Italy, there are 971 women for every 1,000 men; and in Sofia, Bulgaria, there are only 894 women for every 1,000 men. In other cities, such as New York City, there are 999 women for every 1,000 men, and in Chicago, there are 972. Therefore, Europe has become a women's world. This is the result of many men dying on the battlefield during the World War.

A young man in France, named Nasbyde, divorced Miss Huana less than two years after they were married because Miss Huana changed her mind. Because the market had reached a point where it could no longer rise, it was very easy to reverse and fall when the environment changed. As a result, the current month fell by 4.5 cents, December fell by 3.75 cents, January fell by 3 cents, February fell by 3.5 cents, March fell by 3.25 cents, and April fell by 3.5 cents.

The remaining common grades of Jiangsu-Tongnan Port japonica rice are selling slightly less in this street. Medium and secondary grades are also clearly distinguished. The price of early thin rice has fallen by a small amount, a few cents. Yin Yuan is stable, and customer tip rice shows signs of fatigue.

Piece Goods: Fake Horsehair Sleeves Gradually Abandoned: The Influence of the Popularity of Riding Breeches and Coats 274

(Genuine Horsehair Sleeves) Prices have risen sharply yesterday. Domestic Daohua goods are sold at 1.40 yuan, and auction goods are sold at 1.80 yuan. (Fake Horsehair Sleeves) The sales volume in previous years was higher than that of genuine products, but this year it has plummeted. Yesterday, the ordinary brand was uniformly priced at 54-55 cents.

Business Sutra (48): Ge Xian Rice is Cheap 276

Ge Xian rice is produced in Henan and Sichuan, and is a type of fungal plant. It is divided into two types: Xianmi flakes and Xianmi seeds. The texture is similar to that of wood ear, but this one is planted in the soil. Here is a brief description of the goods from Henan and Sichuan for distinction:

Sichuan Xianmi is of better quality. The seeds and flakes are not separated, and the texture is pure and clean, without the problem of sizing. Therefore, it is called "clean water goods". The color is black, like small ears, the flakes are round and flat, and the seeds are rice-shaped. Lower grades are gray in color, but otherwise similar.

Henan Xianmi is of lower quality. The seeds and flakes are packaged separately. Good ones are black in color, while lower grades are green. This is because this product is sized with green vitriol, so the heavier the sizing, the greener the color. Otherwise, they are similar.

For consumption, soak thoroughly in water. It is mostly used for hot stir-fries at banquets, either sweet or savory, plain stir-fried or with a little starch, as desired.

Free Talk

Yuan Zhonglang's Travelogue 277

— Zhu Xia

Although there is no "fixed method" for writing travelogues, in reality, it can be said that there is a kind of "dead method." What is this "dead method"? It is clinging to scenery to write realistically, adding some lyrical feelings, and it must have a beginning and an end, making it a complete article. Throughout the ages, people who write travelogues have been bound by this "dead method" without realizing it, and there have been few new developments. However, Zhonglang's travelogues cannot but be said to be exceptions. The miscellaneous essays in the complete works are all travelogues, and these articles all have a different spirit and a different system. Sometimes, he writes about the current scenery, and sometimes, he does not write a single word about the scenery limited by the topic, only recording his feelings in that place. Sometimes, he writes a few words on a big topic, but he talks at length on a small topic. I think this unique spirit is something that every travelogue writer should learn well. Sticking to the topic and circling around it is, without a doubt, the clumsiest method.

For example, the most widely circulated of Zhonglang's travelogues, "Tiger Hill". For a general writer, of course, the main focus is on narrating the scenery of Tiger Hill, but Zhonglang does just the opposite, using very few words to briefly touch upon the scenery. His focus is on the tourists' mood, writing about the tourists' grand attire, writing about the tourists "setting up wine in the middle of the road", writing about "the accumulation of dirt on the sandalwood clappers, the pouring of wine vessels like clouds", writing about singing, writing about actions, writing about the brightness of the stone, writing about the pens. In this way, not only is the beauty of Tiger Hill more evident, but the "dead" Tiger Hill is also written as "vividly alive". Although he does not write about the scenery of Tiger Hill directly, everything he writes is about Tiger Hill, its scenery, its daytime and nighttime views, its vibrant life. A travelogue, like other writings, can be more powerful if it grasps its center of gravity and writes from the side, sometimes even more so than writing directly. Another example is his "Hundred Flowers Islet" article. He does not write about "Hundred Flowers Islet" directly at all. He only uses a dialogue to explain it. I can quote its full text:

Hundred Flowers Islet is between the Xu and Pan gates. One evening, I went out from Panmen and met Jiang Jinzhi on the road. I asked if the flowers on Hundred Flowers Islet were in full bloom and whether I should go to see them. I said: "There is nothing else, only twenty or thirty dung boats lined up and staggered, the stench is several miles long." Jinzhi laughed and left.

I believe this writing method is the most vibrant, and it is enough to express the author himself in a travelogue. Although he does not write about "Hundred Flowers Islet" directly, the ugly reality under such a beautiful name will give people a deep impression. For example, when he writes about West Lake, the writing method he applies is also the same. He does not write a systematic travelogue of West Lake, but only writes in fragments, and each fragment has its own independent existence that is different from the general. For example, the opening section of "West Lake One": "From Wulin Gate to the west, looking at Baoshu Pagoda, standing out in the middle of the cliffs, my heart has already flown to the lake." From the beginning, it has a special spirit. For example, the topic "Gushan":

The recluse of Gushan, with his plum trees and cranes, is the most convenient person in the world. We are only troubled by so many trivial matters because we have wives. We can't get rid of them, we hate to be near them, like clothes that are worn out and tattered, walking in thorns, worrying about every step. Recently, there is a monk Yu Ru under Leifeng Pagoda who also has no wife. He is probably the reincarnation of Gushan. Although I don't know how his Streamside Falling Flower Poems compare to Lin Hejing, it is said that he can write one hundred and fifty poems in one night, which can be said to be extremely fast. As for eating bland food and practicing Zen, he is even one level higher than Gushan. What era is without extraordinary people!

He simply abandons Gushan and writes about lonely people. There are many other similar examples. For example, the topic "Dragon Well", the focus of his writing is tea. However, Zhonglang is not absolutely opposed to writing about scenery. In many places, he also puts a lot of effort into the scenery. However, he is completely based on necessity; he abandons unnecessary places. We should pay attention to this principle. Among the West Lake articles, there is an article called "Miscellaneous Notes on the Lake", which I think is the best. In the short text, it captures the traces of four months and three trips, which is not easy. However, he still emphasizes writing about life. He also puts effort into depicting things and objects where necessary. There is an article called "Xiang Lake", which is about water shield. Let's look at his "Fishing Terrace" article:

The Fishing Terrace has two stones facing each other, no more than a zhang (unit of length) high. I don't know how many rods he used at that time, or how many pounds of fish he caught. Old Yan is useless, what is the difference between him and this terrace? However, his standing like a wall, looking down on the ruler of men, disregarding the steepness, is also equal to a stone!

This is simply a satirical argumentative essay. In many places, Zhonglang's articles express his own opinions in this way. This is the main feature of his travelogues. The reason why I bring it up is not because I fundamentally oppose narrating scenery in travelogues, but because I advocate that travelogues should have a richer life. If you simply narrate scenery, no matter how wonderful it is, it cannot be considered a living article.

Grandmother's Shriveled Nipples 278

— He Jiahai

In hot weather, Grandmother always wore a pair of shriveled nipples, with one piece of clothing slipped down her back. She bared her chest, blowing wind through her lips while desperately fanning with a wheat stalk fan, dissipating the time in the vegetable garden, the lane, and all the breezy spots nearby. But most of the time, she still liked to sit on that stone bench near the gate, peeling some bean sprouts or twirling some cotton thread. "A guest, a guest!"

I often teased her mischievously like this.

"Don't lie, you won't scare me. What does it matter if a guest comes?"

"They'll laugh at you for being bare-chested!"

"It doesn't matter if an old person is bare-chested."

Seeing me jumping around, she seemed to be very happy, because she often unexpectedly grabbed me, kissed my face, tickled the palm of my hand, and said with a smile:

"Try your grandmother's milk."

"No, no, I want to eat Mum's milk!"

I stubbornly shook my head. Where did milk come from in these shriveled nipples? Mother's milk was plentiful, like a sprinkler, it was not easy to stop once it squirted out.

"Little beast, you will eat my milk one day!"

"Why?"

"Don't ask now, you wait and see."

"Let Dad eat it."

"I want you to eat it!"

I never took this to heart. It was rare for a grandson to eat his grandmother's milk.

But she actually guessed it. One sultry afternoon, Mother suddenly said to me:

"Baby, you have to stop breastfeeding."

"I want to eat!"

"You're standing up so tall now, still eating milk, aren't you ashamed?"

"But I want to eat, Mom!"

"Aren't you afraid people will laugh at you?"

"Eat in the room, people won't see."

I refused to listen, thinking she was teasing me, so not only did I not agree to stop breastfeeding, but I also wanted her to take off her clothes right away and give me a meal right away.

"You really can't eat anymore, look—"

Mother smiled and unbuttoned her clothes, revealing two nipples, which were blood red.

"What is that?"

I asked crying, feeling very disappointed.

"Chili sauce. If you're not afraid of your mouth getting broken from the spice, go ahead and eat!" I cried loudly, wanting to eat several times, but the chili sauce was really scary!

"I'll put chili sauce on it today, and tomorrow I'll put plaster on it. You can eat it if you're not afraid of your mouth getting stuck."

From then on, I didn't dare to bother Mother anymore, and Grandmother's shriveled nipples became my favorite. Because at this time Mother went back to her parents' house to live, my only companion was Grandmother. Although I knew that her shriveled nipples had no milk at all, I touched them all day long, and sucked on them with relish, making clicking sounds; at night, I slept with her, just like I used to hold Mother's nipples every night, I had to hold these shriveled nipples to fall asleep. It seemed that only in this way could I feel satisfied.

"Is there any milk, baby?"

"Not a bit!"

At first, I really felt the boredom of sucking dry nipples, but later I gradually got used to it, and seemed very satisfied.

Human beings are able to "make do" from a young age.

Regarding "Understanding Reality" (Continued) 279

— Xu Maoyong

As for the "Understanding Reality II" essay's argument, I simply find it utterly incomprehensible. First, Mr. Shiheng says the difference between his and my views lies in: I "see the function of art as a camera," while he "sees art as 'the painter's brush, paint, and canvas.'" But he believes my view is mechanical. Let's not discuss whether my view is really as Mr. Shiheng says. Let's look at his own argument: "If an image arises in the painter's mind, even if there is no actual model in front of him, his creation of the character can still be equally real." This is certainly true, but where do the images in the minds of our brilliant painters ultimately come from? If we say that the image is formed based on the memory of an actual model that has been seen, then painting tools and cameras are actually the same. There must be a real object as the subject, but the painter can rely solely on memory when painting and does not need to put the model in front of him. However, when taking a photograph, the object must be in front of you. However, if there is fundamentally no actual thing, then there is no way to take a photo, but is it impossible for a painter's image to arise? Take Sanine, for example. If there were such people in society, then whether it is a camera or painting tools, it can create a portrait of him. But in reality, there is no such person, so even the most skilled photographers and painters cannot create an accurate portrait. So I say: "Tao [the Way] has little to do with artistic creative power." Mr. Shiheng opposes my words. Does he think that if Arzybashev's artistic creative power were higher, he could turn Sanine from nothing into something? Later, Mr. Shiheng added the title of "prophet" to Turgenev, and cited the facts of "Fathers and Sons" as an example. I think it is ridiculous. I believe existence precedes thought. When Turgenev "grasped from reality" the "prototype" of Bazarov, the "prototype" of Bazarov already existed in reality. Others couldn't see it because others' vision was not as "penetrating" as Turgenev's. Turgenev's vision was "penetrating" and saw this prototype before everyone else, so he said it. If he didn't say it, this prototype would still grow, but this growth is due to objective social conditions, not Turgenev's artistic creative power. Mr. Shiheng said that Turgenev "with his artistic expression's accuracy, made this prototype gradually grow, and Russian society eventually produced the type of person that is Bazarov." This simply turns Turgenev into a God whose artistic creative power made Russian society produce Bazarov! Based on this, if Arzybashev cannot create a realistic Sanine type of person for Russian society, then his artistic creative power can be said to be weak!

I have done too little research on literature and art, and it is really presumptuous for me to discuss it with Mr. Shiheng from the standpoint of literature and art. What I hold onto is a little common sense. This common sense makes me believe that artists cannot create a "historical typical figure" with illusory "images," no matter how exquisite their artistic creative power is. I believe that a writer's correct understanding of reality is more important than the correct expression of art. Because, if there is a correct understanding but no correct expression, the "destruction" is like trying to carve a swan but ending up resembling a duck. If the understanding is incorrect but the artistic creative power is too exquisite, then the failure is like trying to draw a dog but ending up resembling a tiger.

Moreover, if something does not exist in reality, where will understanding come from? Where will expression come from?

Two Brothers (42) 280

— By Maupassant, Translated by Li Weike

"Where are you from?"

"Italy."

"From which port?"

"Naples."

Then Pierre seemed to see the fiery plume of Vesuvius in his bewildered eyes, and at the foot of the volcano, in the orange groves of Sorrento or Castellammare, many fireflies flew! How many times had he dreamed of these familiar names, as if he knew the scenery of these places! Ah! He really wanted to leave immediately, no matter where he went, and never come back, never write letters, never let anyone know his situation! No, he had to go back, back to his father's house, to sleep in his own bed.

Forget it, he wouldn't go back; he would wait until dawn. He found the sound of the whistle quite pleasant. He stood up again and began to walk, like a sailor on the night shift walking on the deck.

Another ship followed closely behind the first ship, appearing grand and mysterious. It was an English ship from India.

He also saw several ships coming in, one by one emerging from the deep darkness. Afterward, unable to bear the dampness of the fog, Pierre walked towards the city. He was so cold that he had to go into a coffee shop frequented by sailors to drink a grog (a drink made of hot sugar water, brandy, lemon, etc.); when the spicy and hot brandy burned his throat, he felt a hope again.

Maybe he was wrong? He knew his absurd fantasies very well! He must be wrong? He had accumulated a lot of evidence like someone compiling an indictment to accuse an innocent person of "wanting to add a crime without grounds." When he fell asleep, he would not think like this.

So he went home to sleep, and because he was determined to fall asleep, he finally dozed off.

Five

But the doctor's body only got a couple of hours of paralysis in a very restless sleep. When he woke up in that warm, tightly closed, dark room, before his thoughts even began to move, he felt that painful oppression, that unpleasant feeling after sorrow, which had been temporarily forgotten in his sleep. The disaster that had only bumped into us that night seemed to have slipped into our flesh while we were sleeping, destroying and exhausting us like a fever. Suddenly he remembered again, and he sat up in bed.
