Discussions

Fate 281

— Qin

Because of the second lottery drawing for the aviation highway, the saying of "fate" can be heard everywhere again.

Mother Zhang said: "He is lucky, so he won the first prize."

Sister-in-law Li said: "This was predestined in the previous life, it cannot be forced."

It's true, taking one hope out of five hundred thousand relies on "luck."

Regarding the words "fate," I remember seeing a story in a notebook, the gist of which is this! There was a couple who farmed for a living. The husband strongly believed in fate, and many fortune-tellers said that he was destined to have heavenly wealth, which he also greatly rejoiced in and did not doubt. One day, when he returned from the field, he told his wife that he had discovered a pot of gold ingots on the edge of the field. His wife asked why he didn't take it, and he replied that the fortune-teller had calculated that his fate had "heavenly wealth," and this was "earthly wealth," which he should not have. His wife scoffed at him. Their quarreling words happened to be heard by a neighbor, who rushed to the field to look for it. The so-called pot was indeed there. When he opened it, it was full of small snakes. He was furious, thinking that the couple really intended to make fun of him. So he carried it to their house and, taking advantage of the night, removed the roof tiles of the couple's house and poured the snakes in, shouting, "Heavenly wealth is here!" thinking of repaying them. Unexpectedly, as soon as the snakes were poured down, the couple in bed heard the sound and woke up in surprise, also shouting "Heavenly wealth is here" incessantly. The neighbor on the roof heard a clanging sound when the snakes were poured down, and he was also puzzled. He hurriedly stayed, and only one gold ingot remained in the pot. He couldn't help but laugh, and his chin dislocated as a result. By the time his chin was healed, the ingot was also used up. This story illustrates that everything has "fate." The villager believed that he was destined to get heavenly wealth and did not take earthly wealth, and eventually it was returned to him through the hands of others. The neighbor was not destined to have wealth, so the ingot turned into a snake. In the end, he kept only one, and suffered the pain of a dislocated chin, to punish ordinary people for vainly seeking blessings. This story has spread very widely, and this statement is deeply rooted in people's hearts, and can probably be used as a concrete explanation of the "theory of fate."

Originally, "relying on heaven for food" is the Chinese people's philosophy of life. When rising into the sky, they don't think of taking an airplane, but only hope that a colorful cloud will descend from the sky; when entering the water, they don't create submarines, but only hope that the Dragon King of the Four Seas will invite them; in times of drought, they worship the Dragon King, and in times of flood, they kowtow to the tortoise (recently, the Yellow River flooded, and a large tortoise appeared, and the river workers kowtowed to it, see the Lunyu Half-Monthly). Praying to resist foreign insults, reciting repentance can save the country, all disasters of war, floods, and droughts are all entrusted to fate, hoping that God will save them, and completely abandoning their own efforts. Thus, humans have also become a kind of animal that cannot create or change the environment. Whose fault is this?

But in recent years, the annual fortunes have been very unfavorable. Until this year, the theory that "the Chinese people's bitter fate is already destined" came out, and people's hearts became even more distressed. Fortunately, heaven opened up greatly, and the aviation lottery was issued, allowing the generally disappointed people to slightly recover some hope. Winning the first prize allows one to become a wealthy man with a round face, and even if one does not win the first prize but gets a second prize, one also has the qualification to ride in a car, and jumps out of the "bitter fate." In this way, once every three months (now every two months), each time ten to dozens of people, within a year, I'm afraid hundreds or even hundreds of people escape this "bitter fate" barrier. This is truly a great favor. Although the bitter will become even more bitter because of this, there are always good things. "Try your luck!" This year, everything is originally for fun!

Battlefield Sketch 1 282

— Xiao Peng

After a night of fierce fighting, our army finally advanced victoriously. It was reported that the enemy had fled far away, and the rear baggage team was ordered to follow closely and move forward; some used pack animals, some used ox carts, and some were carried by people. This took a lot of effort to grab using the forced labor method. In the northern weather of the third month of the lunar year, walking is very hot. The desolate wilderness, mountains, and land are covered with military boxes and bedding, especially the soldiers' shouts and roars, also mixed with the "Hangyu" sound of the porters desperately moving forward after being whipped, and the gasping and wailing of the animals rushing around like wild boars. The mighty scene is like a tidal bore in the Qiantang River. After walking about ten miles, we arrived at the place where the fierce battle had taken place the previous night.

Because we hadn't closed our eyes the previous night, and we had rushed on a journey that day, and everyone's stomachs were still so empty, we really needed a proper rest. In this desolate and dilapidated village, in a short while, it turned into a whole gray world. The old folks' things, as long as they could be swallowed, had already been swept away. The women looked on with wide eyes, and men above adulthood couldn't be seen anywhere. Perhaps they had already received the grace of the revolutionary army not forcing labor.

After a while, in a corner of a small thatched hut, a large group of various soldiers crowded together, surrounded layer upon layer, with no water escaping. "Damn your grandmother, death to these old literati..." This sharp scolding sound spread throughout the village. I went closer to take a look. Ah, a headless corpse covered in blood was lying on the ground. Some scattered pieces of flesh adorned this small room, emitting a foul odor. There were also two people in gray military uniforms lying diagonally on both sides, forming a "character 品" shape, their faces pale, white foam coming out of their mouths, bursting with some intermittent and miserable wails: "Help, old... gentlemen!" I immediately felt that these were undoubtedly enemy soldiers who had lost and were unable to retreat.

"I was originally a soldier under Commander-in-Chief X. This time, I was trapped here and didn't have time to withdraw. We are from Shanxi. In the end, that guy (the dead soldier with flesh and blood) became anxious and suggested that we might as well commit suicide first. He called us to gather together, and he detonated the bomb on our heads. He really killed himself, but unfortunately, we only each injured a leg, but we can't walk. Damn him, it's really terrible... Sir, please save us!" Then another tone, with a sad and pleading tone, used all his strength to tremble and complain about their experience in a mournful voice, which of course called us not to hate the enemy and not to end the lives of the two breathing ones.

However, mankind is indeed lacking in compassion. These two wounded brothers of the same class could not ignite their sympathy and warmth, and stubbornly put on a pair of enemy-self colored glasses, disgustingly wanting to beat them. Some raised the guns in their hands, murderously prepared to fire live ammunition, and some even suggested burning them with kerosene. After my painstaking explanation, it was also difficult to break their concept of hating the enemy. The last tragedy was finally staged under the two sounds of "Crack! Crack!" And those two wounded lives were ultimately unfortunately sacrificed under the name of the enemy.

This was an old story from three years ago.

Things to Know When Visiting Friends 283

— Shen Min

If you want to visit a friend; before you set off, you must carefully examine the status and wealth of the friend you want to visit. If that friend's status is higher than yours, you should prepare an attitude of twelve points of respect, and also put on a ninety-eight-degree smile to see him. Especially in conversation, you must pay attention and never reveal a poor state. If you reveal a poor state, then they will suspect that you are asking him for loans. You must know: "Friend" is the transliteration of "碰有" (pèng yǒu), which means "encountering someone who has." If you "have," that's fine. If you don't "have," then how will they treat you as a friend? If you are currently unemployed and want to ask him to arrange a position, or ask him to find a place to eat: then sorry, one hundred and twenty points of sorry! You'd better not open your mouth. Because the important affairs of the general dignitaries and Mr. Tycoons are very busy: their status is very noble: and you are not the brother of their concubine, so how can they arrange a position for you and find a place to eat? If you say the words you want to seek help, not only will they immediately show a very awkward look on their face, but they will immediately be cold to you and hate you. They will go to handle their official business early and not bother you. To put it nicely, they are respectfully declining: to be honest, they are giving you the cold shoulder, so you should ask someone else! You must also keep in mind that when visiting a "noble friend," you must not despise the gatekeeper, because the power to receive guests of his master is all in the hands of the gatekeeper! After you hand over a business card, his honorable eyes will first see what the status of the visitor is, and then he can determine the direction of the reception. If you are an unknown person, they will definitely not immediately convey it to the manager's office. You must not be impatient, patiently, calmly, and respectfully stand aside and wait: after he sends your business card in, he will come out and answer you with a sentence: "The manager is not free." If you are observant and sensible when you are about to leave the office, you should come back early tomorrow! If you are still unlucky tomorrow, you may visit the day after tomorrow. If you are still unlucky the day after tomorrow, you can visit day after day. Anyway, you have nothing to do? You have a lot of time? As for visiting female friends, it is also a very difficult thing? Although women are already free, liberated, and equal between men and women! But the men of our noble country are still stubborn and unchangeable, and most of them are inevitably affected by the Twenty-First Hour of the Western Calendar [a reference to antiquated thinking]. Therefore, sour storms often arise! If you go to a girls' school to visit a female friend, or to some agency or company to visit a beauty, then the servant who specializes in visiting will ask you your last name at the beginning, and who you are visiting: and the second sentence will ask you what you call her! At that time, you will feel difficult to answer. Should you say you are a friend? Or should you say you are a cousin? If you hesitate, sorry, they will give you a cold look and say very angrily: that she is in class or is working.

Wife's Teachings 285

— Meng Yuan

Lately, I have often been taught by my wife.

For example, my getting up late and drinking alcohol have all become the materials for teachings; the beginning of the lecture is always a lightly described sentence, and then this sentence leads to another sentence, and then a problem is brought up in connection, saying endlessly! The final result is either crying or laughing, depending on how I deal with it.

Once, I accidentally talked about my past lover Cui, and inadvertently praised her a few times, but my wife did not say anything at the time; after a while, it seemed that another lecture was coming! Because I praised Cui's few words as a topic, my wife considered it ungentlemanly. Thanks to her for making use of the topic, the lightly described lecture began again:

"I see that you have recently learned to be fashionable and know how to smoke cigarettes!"

For me, it is customary to remain silent and listen attentively. Then, the following comes:

"I really don't understand, taking such spicy things, sucking them in and spraying them out, what does it mean? It won't make you full, so it's better to eat some snacks. And..."

I know that this word "and" means that she is entangled in another problem! So the following:

"Moreover, Cui also smokes, and I don't approve of women smoking the most; if I talk about you, you think I'm slandering her, but sometimes what she does is indeed..."

This pause turns to another question:

"You've been too scheming lately! Smoking is enough! You also want to do other things, and you don't write articles properly. You talk about women and close your mouth about women, and you think about women all day long in your heart."

"Who are you thinking about?" I couldn't help it: "Thinking about you!"

"Who wants you to think about me?" My wife said with righteousness: "I'm not kidding you, I'm worried about you!"

"Don't bother! You are worried about Cui."

"Who is worried about her? What does Cui have to do with me?"

"Cui and you have a big relationship!"

"Okay! I won't talk to you. You have changed now! I advise you and you don't listen; I tell you and you don't listen," so she cried!

After the lecture, I was silent, lowering my head in the dark and chewing on my wife's few words just now.

Waiting to be a Concubine 286

— Jin Jin

Mr. Zhang, who lives at number twenty-two, I heard that he used to be some kind of prefect, and now he has retired to live at home, enjoying a comfortable life. The house is decorated luxuriously, like a palace, full of prosperity. In addition to this mansion, Mr. Zhang also has several small mansions elsewhere, and he spends most of his time lingering in the beautiful concubines' places. This naturally aroused the infinite anger and jealousy of the first wife, but her own age is not young and her beauty has faded. In fact, it is difficult to maintain Mr. Zhang's restless heart. The first wife also knows this, and now she has come up with a strategy to deal with it.

Almost every morning, we can see the maid in Mr. Zhang's mansion coming out to the stove to fetch water, but we haven't seen her come out these past few days. A very pretty girl of thirteen or fourteen has replaced the maid's job. She is very slender and graceful. Although she is only thirteen or fourteen years old, she is already quite charming. Her clothes are also very novel and gorgeous. This makes us very strange, and we can't figure out who she is. If you say she is a newly arrived maid, she would definitely not dress so neatly. If you say she is one of their relatives, you would never ask her to fetch water from the stove. This makes us feel as if we have fallen into a fog, especially my wife, who likes to ask questions, is even more anxious to know the truth. Yesterday afternoon, she saw the maid running into the door, and asked her for news. The maid gently told her, and the mystery was solved.

Shanghai (5) 287

— Zhang Laosan

(9) Such a Foolish Thought

After standing on the balcony for a while, still pondering this question, I inadvertently let a cigarette, barely two puffs taken, slip from my fingers. I glanced at the room next door, where the light was still on. On the delicate window curtain, the shadow of Sister Min was cast, seemingly watching some magazine or something. I picked up a grain of sand from the ground and threw it at the window. The shadow on the curtain gradually enlarged, and after a rustling sound, she poked her head out,

"Can't sleep? Come sit here."

Throwing sand was a mindless act. Since I was bored, I walked over without thinking. Sister Min was wearing a nightgown, revealing her ankles, and sitting on the sofa. A book was lying flat on the small coffee table beside her. I walked closer and saw it was a diary. I vaguely thought I saw my name on it. She patted the other end of the sofa. "Sit down, and don't peek!" she said, standing up and tightening her nightgown. I knew she had misunderstood.

"What's that book?"

I asked, as if explaining.

"A diary. I haven't written in it for a long time."

She took two cigarettes from the small coffee table, handed me one, lit them, and we smiled at each other, already speechless. I crossed my left leg over my right and tried to smoke, experience telling me that in such situations, one cannot remain silent for too long. Sister Min casually closed her diary, but didn't say a word to start a conversation. So I thought of saying something random, but every word stuck in my throat. For example, saying "Aren't you asleep?" when she was clearly sitting on the sofa, was as ridiculous as running into a friend at the cinema and asking "Watching a movie?" The same was true for "Going to kindergarten tomorrow?" since she herself had said that before. The sound of high heels came from the hallway. The Shanghai night was just beginning. I stared blankly at the ceiling, and Sister Min silently swung her bare ankles.

"When you're in love, you might have this kind of feeling," my mind raced onto the track of youth, fantasizing about a scene from a novel. "Why are you silent?" I asked myself, and smiled unconsciously.

"What are you smiling at?"

She thought I had found something laughable about her and asked, startled. I pondered with a smile.

"Such a foolish thought!"

(10) Always Looking Down on Farmers

When I woke up, the sunlight filled the window. The tea boy handed me a note scribbled in pencil on the back of a calendar:

"I rose early, and you were still deep in sweet dreams, so I dared not disturb you. I have gone ahead. Please write to me when you have found a place to settle down. Min."

Her father is a capitalist. He always looks down on us farmers. I heard that when my mother got married, my uncle was firmly opposed. My maternal grandmother, because my mother was meek and virtuous, finally allowed her to marry my father, who was a farmer. Now my mother is dead, and my grandmother is dead. Just like Sister Min said, our relationship has dissipated with the passing of the two elders. I am unwilling to risk great danger and humiliation to see my uncle. Although the newspaper often publishes news about him studying Buddhism recently, it is questionable whether studying Buddhism is to repent for his previous harsh treatment of others. My uncle only has one daughter, and none of his four or five concubines have produced any offspring. His regret is that he has white hair and no son to cherish him. He studies Buddhism hoping that "Heaven" will grant him a precious child. As they say, "When a man is about to die, his words are kind." If the Buddhist scriptures are truly sacred, then like "freedom," many evils in the world are committed in your name. Sister Min holds a great hope for the "future," probably for this reason?

I worried for a long time. It seemed that for Sister Min's fervent hope, I should go to my uncle's house once. It is not my shame that he always looks down on farmers.

In the afternoon, I boarded the Xujiahui tram and took a corner seat. Opening today's newspaper, a headline in the local news column caught my eye: "Philanthropist Xu Bingnan Initiates Buddhist Lecture." Subheading: "Held Today at Fangwai Villa." How unlucky I am to have encountered this event!

Xu Bingnan is my uncle. After building Fangwai Villa last year, he further tricked his way into the title of philanthropist. A Buddhist lecture initiated by a philanthropist naturally needs support, to form good karma! No wonder I waited for several Xujiahui trams, all crowded with people coming and going, like clouds. Never mind what value a Buddhist lecture initiated by a philanthropist has, how do these modern figures have such a strong interest in the Buddhist lecture?

Shanghai, this is how Shanghai has become today!

Film Special

The Basis of Film Criticism 288

— Li Fu

Recently, due to the objective situation in the film industry and the general public's rejection of the formulaic film reviews of the past, there has been a surge in the promotion of constructive film reviews and the exclusive discussion of techniques. Indeed, Chinese film criticism has now reached a very critical moment. If it can rally well at this time and not go astray, then it will certainly be a blessing for the future of Chinese film culture. If we fail to see this imminent crisis clearly and take the wrong path in the first step of re-departure, it may lead the entire film criticism to ruin.

Promoting constructive film reviews and encouraging film critics to further educate themselves more richly are certainly the most crucial tasks at present. However, under these slogans, we must never fantasize that our past ideological criticisms have achieved a successful conclusion. Only because the past film reviews did not follow the right path, being sometimes accommodating, sometimes extreme, and mostly simply using formulas, film criticism lost the trust of the audience and practitioners. From the beginning of film criticism to the present day, the fundamental work of "films are not merely for entertainment! They should have some social significance" has not been fully achieved. Therefore, we must not simply interpret so-called constructive criticism as focusing solely on technical corrections and guidance for films. We must also quickly establish the principles of criticism and strengthen the ideological review of all films.

I believe that the biggest shortcoming of past film criticism was the lack of a definite standard. It is certainly a mistake to criticize Chinese films, which were produced under a distorted development, with overly extravagant standards. Conversely, it is also somewhat comical to demand from the film merchants of the gold-dollar empire principles such as enlightening the public's knowledge and raising cultural standards. Before we criticize a film, we must first recognize under what conditions it was produced. For example, "Iron Heel in Red Shanghai" is a production of the Soviet Union's Sovkino from 1931. Therefore, we have the right to severely criticize its vague analysis of love issues and economic systems. Because it is a work from "1931" in the "Soviet Union." Another example is "42nd Street," which premiered at the Cathay yesterday. This is undoubtedly an American-style film that uses romance and sensuality to attract audiences. However, when we examine it further, we can find that this film is somewhat different from other musicals. Here, there is not only song and dance, not only love entanglements, but it also depicts the inside of a dance troupe, describes the content of so-called stars, and exposes the sorrow behind the joy. Here, we cannot but distinguish these progressive features from the previous works and give a fair critique. To give another example, under the Nazi's iron-fisted politics in Germany, all artists lost their freedom. Therefore, for the works produced under such circumstances, even for the artistic "Dream Lips," we must also express some goodwill towards the artistic conscience of these producers who were not subdued by violence.

What we need is accurate critical standards. To grasp these standards, film critics should strive to understand the current world and society.

Audience Opinions

Impressions of "Scent of Grass Beauty" 289

— Yin Zhong

The content and meaning of "Scent of Grass Beauty" narrates the bankruptcy of our country's industrial factories due to foreign economic aggression, which led to the tragic unemployment of workers who rely on their blood and sweat for a living. In particular, it tells the story of a "young lady" type female worker who, under the pressure of life, had no choice but to sell herself.

The content of such a story can be said to be a true portrayal of real society. At least the structure of this script is more progressive than similar films in the past. The film's presentation is in a "reminiscent" style, which is also a novel method. I remember "Spring Tide" also used this method, but not as "concrete" as here. This may give the audience a new impression. However, some audiences may feel bored, such as the scene where a carpenter who committed a crime due to unemployment narrates the details to the judge in court, which seems too long and too cumbersome. However, the configuration of camera angles is precise, and the rotation is also sensitive and lively.

Speaking of the performances, we must admit that the actors who played the worker Wang Ada and his brother were indeed very successful. Ada's timid expression and his brother's strong character each have different personalities. One is strong and one is timid, which can be said to be "mutually interesting."

In short, this film is already much more impressive than all previous domestic films.

Review of "Scent of Grass Beauty" 290

— Fu Li

The performance of "Scent of Grass Beauty" reveals the terror of economic aggression. Invisibly, a factory could not withstand its pressure and went bankrupt, causing a large number of workers to lose their jobs, affecting social unrest, and producing many tragic and depraved sins.

Regarding the use of this kind of subject matter, as long as it is handled correctly and strictly, it may become a very profound work that is sympathetic to the audience. However, in terms of the performance, the author writes out the entire story in fragments using memories, which inevitably makes the audience unable to see the tense performance in a series. Also, the subtitles with general descriptions are used for every scene change, which also feels too much and too rigid.

The foreign cigarettes displayed in a scene in the window, using "cartoon" paintings to reflect the outflow of money, is very interesting.

Xie Yunqing, who played Wang Ada, was able to fulfill his duties as a character in the play. His facial expressions are also very subtle, even though it was his first time changing his style. Xia Peizhen and Wang Zheng's expressions are also natural, which makes people feel satisfied.

Actor Selection and Makeup – Talking About the Rich and the Foremen 291

— Yan Su

When a director receives a script and wants to start filming, the first important thing is to choose actors that fit the identity and personality of the characters in the play. Secondly, it is also important to pay close attention to how the actors should be made up to suit the characters in the play. This is the most superficial common sense, and no one can deny it. However, I don't know why our Chinese films often use actors who do not fit the identity of the characters in the play to perform. This may be because among all the actors in their company, only that one actor is passable. The second is to focus on star-centrism. As long as he or she is a celebrity who has already become famous, they can attract attention and make money. As for the authenticity of art, it can be ignored. In domestic films, all the rich and landlords are mostly round-faced characters. They probably only know that all the rich and landlords must be round-faced. Secondly, in domestic films, all the foremen and the like are mostly fierce-looking with cross-flesh on their faces. They probably only know that to be a foreman, one must be fierce. Taking the role of the rich man as an example, not long ago, the rich factory owner we saw in "Gold Mountain" and the rich dance troupe boss in "42nd Street" were both successful. The rich factory owner in "Gold Mountain" expressed a kind of weak body and pale appearance, symbolizing the exhaustion of the bourgeoisie in the effort to get rich, but at the same time, he also expressed his domineering and incomparably dignified demeanor. The rich dance troupe boss in "42nd Street," who sponsored the dance troupe for a dancer, expressed a kind of "golden bull" silliness, but he also had his dignity. Speaking of the foreman, the foreman in "Gold Mountain" expressed a kind of treacherousness, cunning, flattery, and meanness, giving people a deep impression of evil-heartedness. Compared with the superficial feeling of fierceness, it is really the difference between heaven and earth.

The Progress of the German Film Industry This Year 292

— Huang Yingdai

The film industry in Germany has been on the rise recently, and judging from the current situation, there are obvious signs of success this year. Since August 1, the film companies have had satisfactory results in terms of production and film rental. In terms of production, credit has been increasing day by day, and a bank for film industry credit loans has also been established. The number of films rented and shown by theaters is also recording new highs. This situation is partly due to the efforts of those engaged in the film industry, but also because Germany's economic situation has recently turned around. The film production plans of the film companies, it is said that until now, all the productions are enough for the next quarter (winter) of Chinese screening. From July to September, the Film Censorship Board passed a total of 66 films, but in the same period in 1931, there were only 54 films, and in the same period in 1931, there were 61 films. The export of German films, from January to August 1933, in the middle of eight months, there were a total of 15,900,000 meters, but in the same period of eight months in 1932, there were 17,900,000 meters. Among the German films transported to various overseas countries, those in German-speaking countries accounted for 42% of the total. From the above, we can easily know that the German film industry is developing very rapidly.

The Script of "Forbidden Garden Spring" is the Same as Fox's Production of "Enchanted Garden" - Janet Gaynor Replaced Lilian Harvey 293

It was probably in July, right? This magazine once published a film novel, originally named Adorable, translated as "Enchanted Garden," produced by Fox and starring Janet Gaynor. At first, I was very surprised why this film has not yet been transported to China for premiere, but now I understand.

It turns out that the script for this film produced by Fox was purchased from the German Ufa company. It was rumored last year that Ufa and Fox were cooperating, which is also one reason. However, all the copyrights owned by Fox are limited to the United States. Therefore, the film "Enchanted Garden" can only be premiered in the United States, while Ufa company simultaneously used this script to film a film called Her Highness Commands, translated as "Forbidden Garden Spring." The content is all the same as "Enchanted Garden," but the title has been changed, and the actors have been changed. In this film, Lilian Harvey plays a princess of noble descent, while also disguising herself as a petite and exquisite maid. It is not easy to make the identities of the two different characters so similar. This is undoubtedly another new type of musical film with a very humorous court romance. The left is a scene from "Forbidden Garden Spring."

Film Novels Win Glory for the Country (3) 294

— Xie Yuesheng

Xuefang and Surong were chatting idly when they suddenly saw Hongyu Tianxiong come in. She quickly got up to greet him and introduced Surong to him. Hongyu, seeing Surong's outstanding talent and appearance, and his graceful demeanor, had already expressed her infinite enthusiasm to him in her heart.

Under the shady willow trees, sat a pair of young lovers. In the green and oily waves, reflected their beautiful figures. Xuefang nestled in Surong's arms, mutually intoxicated in the deep abyss of love.

Suddenly, Surong was suspected of some political offense. One-five-ten, they dragged Surong to the police station. This surprised Xuefang so much that her soul flew to the ninth heaven. She hurriedly begged Tianxiong to help Surong get out of prison. On a night when gray shrouded the earth, Cheng Tianxiong discovered this surprising XX mystery case from a quiet secret cave. He heard Cao Huairen and his accomplices plotting to frame Surong. He quickly reported to the detective team, but the alert Cao Huairen escaped before their partisans were arrested. Mei Xuefang, to thank Tianxiong for rescuing Surong, specially held a celebration party.

Time passed day by day, and the feelings between Su and Mei grew day by day. Cao Huairen, who was wealthy and powerful, of course could not make him feel peaceful and submissive. He had previously built a secret room in the countryside, waiting for Xuefang and Surong to come out to play, intending to imprison them in the mechanism, to avenge the previous failure.

Mei's mother, because Xuefang and Surong were missing at the same time, hurriedly invited Tianxiong to come home to discuss. Tianxiong understood the cause of the mystery case and, relying on his mysterious means, discovered Cao Huairen's mechanism. He comforted Mei's mother while inviting his father and sister to rescue Su and Mei. "Don't you like the surname Su?" Cao Huairen said to Xuefang in a threatening manner. He shouted as the henchmen whipped Surong, and a sinister beauty floated on his frightening mask. This could not help but surprise Xuefang and make her scream. Then, there was a burst of gunfire and noise, and Cao Huairen was knocked to the ground. Tianxiong and Hongyu, along with his father, Cheng Dapeng, rescued Surong and Xuefang.

Xuefang was grateful for Tianxiong's rescue and admired his courage, rekindling the fire of love. "Mr. Cheng, thank you for saving me several times, I am so grateful, how can I repay you in the future?" She said shyly, with a smile, slowly lowering her head towards Tianxiong. "No, Xuefang: I don't want you to thank me, I feel that I want to..." Tianxiong knew that these words were too abrupt, and the blood in his whole body was so tense that it seemed about to collapse. "Xuefang, I love..." This sentence containing sulfurous words finally exploded in Tianxiong's fiery emotions. (To be continued)
